Opening of London Art Exhibition - British Official Sends Congratulatory Telegram - Chairman Lin Responds, Telegram Forwarded by British Embassy

(Nanjing) The London International Exhibition of Chinese Art has officially opened in the British capital. This office has received a congratulatory telegram from the exhibition's Chairman, Lord Lee of Fareham, and Vice-Chairman, Lord Willingdon, forwarded by the British Embassy in China to Chairman Lin of the National Government. A reply, drafted in the name of the Chairman, was immediately sent to the British Embassy in China for transmission to London, so that the British government could have it read at the banquet it is hosting for the exhibition this month, in March. The original telegram is as follows: (1) "The International Exhibition of Chinese Art is being held at the Royal Academy of Arts in London. Your government's participation is greatly appreciated. We, on behalf of all British artists and art lovers, extend our sincere thanks to your Chairman. We believe it is especially important that the artistic genius of your country is thus displayed before Western art. We are confident that this exhibition will promote cultural communication and mutual understanding between our two countries." - Lord Lee of Fareham, Lord Willingdon. (2) "Having just received the congratulatory telegram informing me that the International Exhibition of Chinese Art has officially opened at the Royal Academy of Arts in London, I, as Chairman, extend my warm congratulations to Your Excellencies, and through Your Excellencies, to the British artists and art-loving people. I, as Chairman, firmly believe that this exhibition will broaden the scope of appreciation for Chinese art and deepen understanding of the mutual relationship between Eastern and Western cultures. This represents a new expression of Sino-British cooperation and serves as further proof of the friendship between the two countries. I, as Chairman, hereby express my sincere gratitude on behalf of the Chinese people to all those involved in holding the exhibition." - Lin Sen. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

The King and Queen of England Visit the Chinese Antiquities Exhibition - Guided by Guo Taiqi and Zheng Tianxi

(London) This afternoon, the King and Queen of England, accompanied by their daughter-in-law, the Duchess of Kent, paid a private visit to the Chinese art exhibition at Burlington House. They were greeted by the Chinese Ambassador, Guo Taiqi, the President of the Royal Academy of Arts, Sir William Llewellyn, and Dr. Zheng Tianxi, the commissioner for the exhibition appointed by the Chinese government. Also in attendance were Princess Louise, Princess Victoria, and Lady Ramsay. The party toured the various rooms for an hour and a half, expressing great appreciation for the exhibits. During the visit, they were guided by Dr. Zheng Tianxi and Lord Lee of Fareham. The renowned art expert Sir Percival David also explained the origins of many of the exhibits to the distinguished guests. The King and Queen inquired about how such delicate items could be safely transported from China to England. Sir Percival David explained that special crates were made in Shanghai for transportation. The Queen wished to see these crates, so she was led to them. The guests were very interested. As the King passed through the rooms, he repeatedly praised the proper arrangement of the exhibits and the pleasing appearance of each room. The Queen also praised the effective display of the selected exhibits. As the King and Queen traveled by car from Buckingham Palace to the venue, the crowds cheered for them along the way. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) At a banquet held today by the Royal Central Asian Society to celebrate the International Exhibition of Chinese Art at Burlington House, Chinese Ambassador Guo Taiqi stated that the Chinese government's sending of precious artifacts to the exhibition was an expression of goodwill from the entire Chinese nation. He added that the British public's enthusiastic appreciation of the exquisite beauty of Chinese art had richly rewarded this goodwill, which he found gratifying. Ambassador Guo also said that this exhibition demonstrated the international cooperation and sincere collaboration among many government and private collectors, enhancing the value of art and promoting the spirit of art. Chinese art, spanning over three thousand years, is a symbol of creativity. China, in the midst of unprecedented difficulties, is still able to strive for national revival, relying on this creativity to inspire its spirit, he stated. Renowned scholar, author, and speaker Mr. Laurence Binyon also delivered a speech, predicting that a large museum of Asian art would be established in London, collecting art from India, Persia, Turkestan, China, Japan, and scattered throughout the world under one roof. There, one could witness the central and superior position of Chinese art and its traditions. Binyon then praised the renowned art expert Sir Percival David, saying that without Sir David's initiative, this exhibition could never have been realized, and that the French Oriental scholar Paul Pelliot also contributed greatly. (Reuters, 2nd)

Japanese People Cause Trouble Drunk in Tianjin

(Tianjin) On the 2nd, a Japanese man named Nishimura came to Tianjin from Guye. In the British Concession, he shouted slogans such as "Realize the autonomy of North China" and "East Asian peace". He then took out a pistol and loaded it in the street. Fearing that people would see him, he entered the nearby Victoria Hospital. A nurse at the hospital saw him and asked what he was doing. Nishimura fired a shot into the air and chased the nurse upstairs, causing chaos in the hospital. Several American doctors worked together to seize the gun, resulting in a physical struggle. Nishimura then took out a dagger and attempted to stab them. A large number of British police officers arrived and arrested him. According to his statement, he had just arrived in Tianjin from Guye and intended to enter the Japanese Concession, but a misunderstanding occurred due to drunkenness. The British Municipal Council has protested to the Japanese Consulate. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

International Commercial Telegraph - Reuters Special Commercial Report for December 2nd

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today is 141 shillings, down half a penny.

British Silver: The London silver spot price rose by 0.0625 to 29.25 pence. Futures remained unchanged at 28.875 pence. Purchases from America, sales from the East, and the market price is stable.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning with little fluctuation. The opening exchange rate for British-American currency was $4.9325, which is 0.125 lower than the closing rate on Saturday and Sunday. An hour later, it rose by 0.0625, and at noon, it fell to $4.930625, with no further changes thereafter.

British-French: The opening price rose by 6 points to 74.90 francs. Before noon, it fell by 5 points to 74.85 francs.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The cotton market opened with some buying due to a shortage of sellers, but then it became quiet. Prices did not change, and trading was sluggish because operators were unwilling to trade much before the announcement of cotton field figures.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened down 0.25, and then continued to fall due to liquidation by bulls. The trend of coarse grains was the same as that of wheat.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was quiet this morning. At 1 p.m., the December futures price was 6 shillings and 0.0625, unchanged.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was slightly loose today. At 1 p.m., the February futures price rose by 3 points to 6.39.

Rubber

New York: The weakening of the London rubber market price caused a large number of bulls to liquidate in the New York market, causing prices to plummet across the board. However, buying by peers later caused prices to rebound slightly.

London: The rubber market was flat this morning. The opening price for April and June futures was 6.5 pence, the same as the closing price on Saturday. At noon, it fell by 0.125 to 6.375 pence.

Securities

New York: The stock market opened this morning, and prices fell almost across the board due to the instability of the European situation. Mining stocks fell the most, while oil stocks and utility stocks were slightly higher. After half an hour, the market showed a stable appearance. The average opening price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks was 142.31, down 4 points.

The British Empire News Agency - London Builds Nine-Story Mansion - Grand Scale and Perfect Equipment - Reuters and the Associated Press Cooperate Closely - A New Era of World News Exchange Opens

London Dispatch: A large building is about to be built on Fleet Street in London for Reuters News Agency and the British Associated Press. All British Empire and foreign communication agencies related to Reuters, as well as newspaper agencies that have direct contact with the Associated Press, will also be included. This will be the largest and best-equipped news exchange location in the world. The design of the new building was planned by Sir Edwin Lutyens.

Twelve years ago, Reuters in London expanded its business, and its original century-old building could not accommodate it. Therefore, the general management department and the international news department were moved to a new building near Blackfriars. At that time, the location felt quite spacious and had plenty of room for expansion. However, in less than a few years, the business increased day by day, and the old and new locations were no longer sufficient to meet its needs. Therefore, there was a proposal to build a new mansion, not only to merge the two offices into one, but also to include its British Empire and foreign communication agencies.

At the same time, the British Associated Press was also facing similar difficulties. Its current location at Byron House has become too crowded and insufficient for use. It had no choice but to move to a better location. The Associated Press was established 70 years ago. It initially used British Empire and foreign news from Reuters, so the relationship between the two parties was close and long-standing. Later, the relationship became even closer. Both parties' leaders adopted a policy of active cooperation without hindering their respective scopes of activities or losing their distinct personalities. Reuters is a British Empire and foreign news agency, while the Associated Press is the responsible general agency for domestic news gathering.

It was a natural result for the two parties to join hands to deal with the difficulty of finding premises. Therefore, they tried to purchase the land behind Byron House so that it would be connected to Byron House, reaching Salisbury Court from Fleet Street. At the same time, they hired architect Sir Edwin Lutyens to design and draw the plans. The purchase of the new land and the preparation of the drawings took nearly a year. Now, Byron House and its neighboring buildings are about to be demolished.

The new nine-story building faces the street on all four sides. The main entrance is located on Fleet Street. Inside, there will be the latest receiving and transmitting news equipment, as well as several inventions that have been studied for a long time. Reuters and the Associated Press will jointly operate and exchange news in the new building in the closest cooperation. This will allow the Associated Press to serve all British newspapers with high efficiency, and Reuters to serve the British Empire, Europe, the Far East, and other parts of the world with high efficiency.

British overseas communication agencies and foreign communication agencies related to Reuters will all have their London offices located in this new building. The continuous stream of domestic and foreign news received by Reuters and the Associated Press in 48 hours every day can be distributed to various offices at any time, so that news from all over the world can be transmitted quickly and spread around the world without delay.

In short, after the new building is completed, the system will be new, the working methods will be different from before, and a new era of world news cooperation and exchange will begin. (Reuters)

(Nanjing) In October, the Nanjing Xiaguan Station approved the Jiao Tong Company to obtain 40 licenses for car operations at the station, and the license fees were paid until the end of December. After mediation by the military police, at about 2 p.m. on the 2nd, both companies sent cars to the station again. The Inheritance Tax Regulations Have Been Drafted

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance, in order to open up legitimate tax sources and increase national treasury revenue, has drafted both income and inheritance tax regulations. The draft income tax regulations have been prepared and submitted to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Central Political Committee for review and approval. Currently, because the income tax and the taxes collected by the central government seem to have overlapping properties, a solution is being sought. The inheritance tax regulations have also been drafted and will be sent to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Central Political Committee. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Education has formulated temporary measures for the establishment of vocational guidance groups in the educational administrative agencies of various provinces and cities and ordered them to be set up and reported on the 2nd. The main points of the measures: (1) In addition to setting up the group, a committee for higher education and vocational guidance should also be organized. (2) The group should be divided into four sections: documentation, introduction, research, and promotion. (3) The group's scope of work includes ten items: implementation, guidance, investigation, occupation, counseling, and acting as an agent for recruitment examinations for various schools. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Japanese Troops Enter the Pass One After Another - Building a Large Airfield in Tianjin - Can Accommodate 70 Aircraft

Tianjin Dispatch: North of the Wan Guo Racecourse in Juzi, Dongju, Tianjin, there is a piece of open space belonging to the Beining Railway Bureau, about 700-800 mu. It is not known when it was investigated by the North China White Garrison Army. It intends to borrow it as a temporary airfield and expand it to the north, wanting to occupy 600 mu of land in Tianjin County. Initially, Major Dohyaku Mitsuo, a staff officer of the unit, went to see Chen Zhongyue, the magistrate of Tianjin County, and requested to borrow it, but Chen politely refused. Unexpectedly, on November 26, a team of about 60 soldiers from the Kwantung Army Air Force came from outside the pass. After getting off the train, they were sent to the aforementioned location, occupied it by force, and engaged in surveying. On the 27th, the Japanese army in Tianjin found more than 200 workers and transported rollers and other materials to start leveling. The Japanese surveyors occupied a part of the Wan Guo Racecourse building as a temporary garrison. Two mat sheds were built on the leveled ground for workers to rest. On the 28th and 29th, nearly one-third of the leveling was completed, and suddenly the nearby civilian land was occupied, expanding the ground to more than 3,000 mu. All the late rice planted in the farmland was removed. The workers were also increased by hundreds, speeding up the construction. Although there was heavy snow on the 30th, they still braved the wind and cold to level. The households whose land was occupied appealed to the Tianjin County Government, and the county magistrate forwarded it to the provincial government. Shang Zhen specially ordered Chen Dongsheng, the counselor of the provincial government's Tianjin office, to visit Tada, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, and Kawagoe, the Japanese Consul General in Tianjin, to negotiate. Tada and Kawagoe said that it was a temporary loan and would be returned soon. However, after meeting twice, they could not get any results. Therefore, they can only let them build for the time being. According to military observers, the ground occupies more than 3,000 mu, and at least 50 aircraft can land at the same time. Adding the airfield built in front of the Balitai Okura Farm, if about 70 aircraft come to Tianjin, they can all be parked comfortably. Since the discovery of a fake people's movement in Tianjin on the 25th, Japanese aircraft have been flying over the city continuously from morning to night, or investigating the situation outside the city. Several aircraft were parked at the Balitai airfield, flying back and forth every day, picking up and dropping off senior Japanese military officers, which was very busy. The tense situation makes the people of Tianjin uneasy.

The North China Japanese Army stationed in Shanhaiguan and the Japanese Army in Tangshan Luanxian are all under the command of Tada. Since the 26th, they have successively opened up to Pingjin. The Beining East Section left behind is taken over by the newly arrived Japanese Kwantung Army. The North China Garrison Army totals more than 1,600 people. The Matsui Brigade, which opened up from Shanhaiguan, reached about 5,000 people. On November 29 and 30, soldiers from the Suzuki Brigade took 17 trains and opened up to Yuguan. Eight of these trains have stopped at Yuguan Station, and the other nine trains are currently stopped at the East Station in the former section outside the pass because there is no housing to live in inside the pass. They can open up into the pass in about one or two days. In the direction of Gubeikou, the Kawagishi Brigade has repeatedly increased, and a regiment has arrived. Xifengkou and Malanyu also have increases. The Japanese side plans to transfer a division and a brigade of the Kwantung Army into the pass and arrange them at various passes of the Great Wall within a week. Including the North China Garrison Army, the total number of soldiers reaches more than 18,000 people. Starting on the 30th, the Japanese army in Tianjin has been looking for houses near Ningyuan, which are suitable for stationing 3,000 people. They went to inspect the old rear defense hospital of the 51st Army, but they did not decide because the houses were broken and dilapidated. They are still looking for them. (1st) (Hai)

Suzhou - Silver Industry Argues About Silver Fineness

The Wuxian Gold and Silver Industry Association, in view of the report that the Ministry of Finance stipulates that the silver used by silver shops in silver ornaments must be 7 parts of copper, if implemented, will be very related to the credibility of the industry and will greatly affect the business. A meeting was held recently to discuss this issue. All members expressed dissatisfaction and decided to request the Ministry of Finance to provide relief to maintain the business and credibility, and to continue to use pure silver. It is heard that the Changshu County Gold and Silver Industry also has this view and has submitted it to the Ministry for relief, still using pure silver.

Ningbo - Shenjiamen Will Have a Market

The fishermen and merchants of Dinghai Shenjiamen, in view of the fact that the fisheries in Zhejiang Province have been declining year by year, believe that the reason is the reduction in production and the narrow sales channels. Therefore, they plan to set up a fish market in Shen in the short term. When it is realized in the future, it will be linked with the Shanghai Fish Market. The price of fish can be increased, which will not only benefit the fishermen greatly, but also give the fish industry a surplus and increase its external credit. It can also be used to borrow loans to help the fisheries, increase production, and be effective. It is a win-win situation.

Nanchang Jiangxi Donation Supervision Committee Chairman Xu Suzhong Requests Resignation

Xu Suzhong, Chairman of the Donation Supervision Committee of this province, recently telegraphed the Executive Yuan, saying, "To the esteemed Wang, President of the Nanjing Executive Yuan: I, Suzhong, am dull and have long abandoned hope of distinction. Unexpectedly, Your Excellency's esteemed Yuan mistakenly adopted undeserved praise and appointed me as a member of the Jiangxi Donation and Tax Supervision Committee. I was perplexed for months, fearing I would be unable to fulfill the task. Later, due to the earnest urging of the provincial government and the eager expectations of the people, I reluctantly heeded the loyal advice of my colleagues and jointly planned the establishment of the committee. Unexpectedly, I received excessive affection and was undeservedly granted the position of Chairman. The responsibility is great and the task heavy, making me feel even more inadequate. Since taking office, although relying on the cooperation of my colleagues, I have fortunately avoided failure. However, because I also hold the concurrent positions of President of the Shanghai Jiangxi Advanced Vocational School and Shanghai Jiangxi Middle School, I cannot reside at the committee permanently and devote myself to my duties. Reflecting on myself, I realize that I have made many mistakes. Recently, the Ministry of Education promulgated the Middle School Law and the Vocational School Law, both of which stipulate that school principals shall not hold concurrent positions. I should respectfully comply with these regulations to avoid dereliction of duty. I earnestly request Your Excellency to approve my resignation from the position of Jiangxi Donation and Tax Supervision Committee member so that I may dedicate myself to education and seek ways to repay your kindness in the future. This telegram expresses my eagerness to await your command." Xu Suzhong bows respectfully.

Scientific Miscellany

— Edited by the Science Society of China

The Moon Returns to Mother's Embrace (Part 2)

— Zhang Yuzhe

From this, we can see that the Earth is indeed the Moon's mother. It is likely inevitable that there will be a feeling of separation from the distant horizon. Once the bright moon falls, it can be considered a wanderer returning home, which should slightly console the mother's longing gaze at the village entrance. Especially among the many satellites, the Moon is remarkably plump. If the Sun could enjoy the joy of having grandchildren, the Moon would surely be one of its most favored. Jupiter, the Sun's eldest son, weighs less than one-thousandth of his mother's weight. Jupiter has nine children surrounding his knees, and the weight of his largest child is only about one ten-thousandth of Jupiter's. The weight of the eldest child in Saturn's family is only one four-thousandth of Saturn's. However, our Moon weighs as much as one-eightieth of the Earth's weight, so it can naturally be considered an outstanding grandchild. Because the Moon has this particularly plump physique, we suspect that the "surgery" it underwent when it was born was slightly different from that of other satellites. According to the opinion of Darwin's great-grandson, the originator of the theory of evolution, the Moon was produced when the Earth had not yet solidified and was rotating very rapidly, coupled with the tidal effect of the Sun, and was split off from the Earth's body. At that time, the Earth was still a liquid, so it would be stirred up by the Sun into a towering peak. When the peak broke off, its upper end solidified into the Moon, which was already very far away from the Earth. However, compared to the current distance between the Moon and the Earth, it was only one-twenty-fourth.

So why did the Moon leave the Earth and run farther and farther away? Is it because it has a wandering nature? Upon investigation, the tides in the ocean cannot escape blame. The Earth is rotating, and the tides are always hindering it. Back then, the Earth could rotate once in just four hours. How agile that was! Now it takes twenty-four hours to rotate once. But waxing and waning are unavoidable phenomena in nature. As the Earth's rotation slowed down, the Moon's orbit around the Earth became more and more energetic. The Earth's control over the Moon had to be gradually relaxed, allowing it to go further and further away. However, when the time it takes for the Earth to rotate once is equal to the time it takes for the Moon to orbit the Earth once, then things will take a turn for the better. At that time, only one side of the Earth will be able to raise a glass to invite the bright moon, while the people on the other side will not even recognize the Moon. It is not yet known which hemisphere will have the good fortune of embracing the bright moon for eternity. Thinking carefully about this good fortune, although it is not a blank check, it will inevitably be greatly discounted in the future. Because the Moon is running farther and farther away, its clear radiance will surely be far less than it is now.

It is said that at that time, the duration of a day and night and a synodic month will be approximately equal to the current forty-seven days. From then on, the behavior of the tides will completely change its past mistakes. It will no longer be a drag on the Earth, but will help push the Earth to speed up its rotation. Then, according to the principle of waxing and waning (in scientific terms, it is called the conservation of angular momentum), the speed of the Moon's orbit will gradually slow down. Thus, this wanderer who has been away from home for a long time will have to gradually throw himself into the embrace of his loving mother. From the Moon's perspective, this action can be regarded as an expression of filial piety. People who advocate loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, harmony, and peace should encourage it. However, this stone ball, equivalent to thousands of towering mountains, falling from mid-air, the people in the world will either be crushed to death or shaken to death. I am afraid that even moralists will hardly be spared to convey people's approval to the Moon.

Fearing that someone will accuse me of starting with rumors and ending with rumors, I must quickly declare here that when the Moon is about to fall to the Earth, a savior will surely appear to erase this great calamity of mankind in one stroke. However, it is difficult to have both. Although this savior is a blessing to mankind, the Moon will inevitably suffer. Because the Earth also has the power of tidal forces on the Moon. Relying on its more robust physique, when the Moon is too close to it, the Earth's power can gradually tear the Moon apart, turning it into countless small moons, flying around the Earth, and no longer crashing down. If you don't believe this, please look up at Saturn. Is he as fortunate as Jupiter? He also has nine satellites orbiting him. However, closest to Saturn's side are not moons, but several extremely beautiful rings (the naked eye needs a telescope to see them). These rings are none other than examples of satellites that have been crushed to pieces. If our Moon is wise, it should know to take this as a warning. According to mathematical estimates, the Moon was born about 4 billion years ago. But from now until the bright moon returns to Earth's embrace, the age to be passed is more than just a fleeting moment of these 4 billion years. If we want to admire the grand spectacle of the future when many moons cover the sky, then we must follow in the footsteps of the Qin Emperor and pursue the method of immortality.

Page 9

Opera Star Yandong Returns to the Stage After Recovering from Asthma, Her Beauty is More Exquisite, and Her Nightingale-Like Voice Lingers Around the Beams

At a singing competition in a certain city not far from Shanghai, there were more than a dozen opera stars. Among them, Yandong was the mainstay, because she had both a beautiful appearance and excellent singing skills. Unexpectedly, Yandong was careless in her daily life a while ago, which led to a cold. At first, her throat became inflamed, then she coughed slightly, and finally she developed asthma. As a result, she could not go on stage to sing clearly. The regulars of the club were very disappointed and did not go to the club to listen to the opera. As a result, the business plummeted. Later, Yandong sought medical treatment in Shanghai. The doctor advised her to take "Medical Lung Star" tablets, a British medicine for asthma sold by the China Merchant Xinhua Company Manager. The effect was indeed rapid and miraculous. Recently, her cough has completely stopped, her throat sound can be said to be completely restored, and her jade face is even more exquisite. The owner of the club heard this and asked her to repeat the performance. Yandong returned to the stage the other day and sang as usual. Her nightingale-like voice turned, and the lingering sound reverberated around the beams. The audience responded with enthusiastic applause for as long as three minutes. Yandong was encouraged by this and sang even more energetically. In recent days, the club has been so crowded that there is almost no room to stand.

"Medical Lung Star" tablets are specially designed to treat asthma and bronchitis cough. It is suitable for both the elderly and children. For detailed instructions, please write to China Merchant Xinhua Company, 367 Jiangxi Road, Shanghai. (Six)

Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau's Simple Life Insurance Officially Opened Yesterday, Over 300 Guests Arrived to Congratulate, Leaders from All Walks of Life Joined the Insurance

The simple life insurance business of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau officially opened on December 2nd. From 10:00 AM, the Bureau's front was bustling with guests arriving in an endless stream. Those who went to congratulate from all walks of life included Sir Frederick Maze, Inspector General of Customs, Zheng Lai, Director of the Customs Administration, Lin Jinyu, Director of the Audit Office, Huang Boqiao, Director of the Two Roads Bureau, Xu Yuanfang, Director of the General Affairs Department, Bao Keyong, Director of the Telegraph Bureau, Xu Xueyu, Director of the Telephone Bureau, Wen Yuqing, Director of the Telecommunications Bureau, Wu Qiding, Director of the Tax Bureau. From the banking sector, there were Tang Shoumin, Chen Guangfu, Xu Xinliu, Zhu Ziliang, Lin Kanghou, Yang Yinsun, and from other sectors, there were Hu Yongqi, Mu Ouchu, Liang Chenlan, Liu Jingshan, Zhao Yuntai, Ding Xuenoong, Li Sihao, etc., as well as yesterday's Shanghai Postal Administration Director Pei Lin. They all arrived one after another. The Director of the Bureau, Shen Shuyu, the Deputy Directors, McLaren and Zhou Shouliang, accompanied them. The reception room was crowded and bustling, reaching a peak for a while. A total of about 300 guests came. Leaders from all walks of life who joined the insurance to promote it included Lin Kanghou, Chen Guangfu, Xu Xinliu, Song Ziliang, Mu Ouchu, Huang Boqiao, Wu Qiding, Ding Xuenoong, Liu Jingshan, Wang Zhixin, Hu Yongqi, Shen Yangyi, etc., as well as the Director of the Bureau, Shen Shuyu, the Deputy Director, Zhou Shouliang, and the Directors of various departments, secretaries, and Bureau members, dozens of people in all. There were also many outsiders who went to the Bureau to join the insurance. This national business is beneficial to society and has four characteristics: (1) Simple insurance procedures; (2) Low premiums; (3) No medical examination required; (4) People are sent to collect fees. As for the difference between simple life insurance and ordinary life insurance, ordinary life insurance calculates the premium based on the insured amount, while simple life insurance calculates the amount based on the premium, which is the opposite. It is hoped that people from all walks of life and the general public will work together to promote and join the insurance. Given the vastness of our country's territory and the large number of people, if it is promoted nationwide in the future, the results should not be difficult to surpass those of Europe, America, and Japan.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Expands the Business Committee, the Revival Association's Affairs Have Ended, Soliciting Opinions on Industrial Relief

Xinsheng News Agency reported that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Industry and Commerce Revival Committee has solved the issue of chips along with the currency reform. The revival of industry and commerce after this lies in practical facilities, and there is no need to design institutions to conduct theoretical research. A resolution was passed at the Fourth Committee Meeting to end it, and it was approved by the Chamber of Commerce's Standing Committee. The association has stopped working as of November 30th, and all unfinished matters will be taken over by the Chamber of Commerce. The details are recorded as follows:

Ministry of Finance Sends Letters to Various Courts, Please Severely Punish Smugglers of Silver Bullion, Buying Privately at High Prices, Intending to Smuggle and Evade Export

The Ministry of Finance has repeatedly received confidential reports that there are unscrupulous people in this city who are privately buying silver coins and silver types at high prices, intending to smuggle and evade export, and with the approval of the municipal authorities, many cases have been reported and sent to the court for trial. Yesterday, the local court, the First and Second Special Zone Courts, were specially requested to severely punish them in accordance with the law. The original letter is as follows: "Article 1 of the measures for implementing legal tender announced and implemented by the Ministry on the 4th of this month states, 'From November 4th of this year, the banknotes issued by the Central, China, and Transportation Banks will be designated as legal tender. All receipts and payments of food, taxes, and all public and private funds will be limited to legal tender. Cash cannot be used. Violators will have all of their money confiscated to prevent the smuggling of silver. If there is any intentional hoarding or concealment with the intention of smuggling, they should be punished in accordance with the Emergency Punishment Law for Harming the Republic of China,' etc. In addition, the Ministry formulated eight measures for exchanging legal tender, all of which were submitted to the Executive Yuan for submission to the National Government for compliance and announcement on file. Recently, confidential reports have repeatedly been received that in the Shanghai area, there are unscrupulous people who are privately buying silver coins and silver types at high prices, intending to smuggle and evade export, and with the approval of the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Public Security Bureau has reported that many cases have been seized and sent to the court for trial. These criminals, at this time of financial crisis and serious national crisis, dare to violate laws and regulations, engage in private gain, and disrupt social economy and endanger national survival. Your court is requested to severely punish them in accordance with the law to warn those who are treacherous and to provide for prevention. I hereby send this letter, and I hope that you will check it out."

Transfer of Association Affairs Separately

The Association's affairs are most focused on investigation and training. The investigation work has been transferred to the Business Section for takeover. The training work includes the establishment of a research class on practical problems in industry and commerce, which was originally co-organized with the Commercial Night School. The speakers are all experts, and the results are excellent. It is now completely taken over by the Night School. All personnel transferred from various departments have also returned to their original positions in their respective departments to work.

Expand the Business Committee

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that the members of the Revival Association are very enthusiastic about their past work, and all reforms in business in the future still need to rely on them. It has been decided to expand the organization of the Business Committee and add the original expert members of the Revival Association, Pan Xulun, Xu Yongzuo, Zhang Naiqi, Pan Yangyao, Li Wenjie, Xi Yushu, Yang Yinpu, Shou Yicheng, Cai Chengxin, He Qingru, Wang Xiaowen, and Xu Xiaochu, and 16 other people to the Business Committee in order to gather ideas and benefit from them.

Soliciting Opinions on Relief

The Chamber of Commerce, based on the letter from the Shipping Industry Association, believes that the depression of industry and commerce, taking advantage of the currency reform, is the only opportunity for economic revival. It should request the government to quickly implement the establishment of special banks and determine the minimum interest rate to avoid missing the opportunity. In addition to immediately submitting it to the Ministry of Finance, the Chamber of Commerce sent letters to various industries to solicit opinions for compilation and handling.

Public Security Bureau Thoroughly Eliminates Opium; Opium Dens Within the Territory Must Close by a Deadline; Those Discovered After the Deadline Will Be Punished According to Military Law; Extensive Publicity Urges Opium Addicts to Repent

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau began the mandatory registration of opium addicts, which will end at the end of this month, the bureau, determined to eliminate opium, began a second round of investigations yesterday. It is scheduled to conduct a joint land and water operation from the 5th, with strict investigations. All privately established opium dens within the territory must close by the end of the month. Those discovered after the deadline will be punished according to military law. Our reporter has learned the following details:

Strict Land and Water Operation

To complete the registration of opium addicts and thoroughly eliminate opium, the bureau began its second round of investigations yesterday. Starting the day after tomorrow (the 5th), the staff of the Opium Addict Registration Section of the bureau, together with police officers from various district offices and water patrol police, will be fully mobilized to conduct district-by-district investigations. Once discovered, offenders will be punished according to the promulgated regulations and ordered to register. Those unable to pay the fines will be sent to drug rehabilitation centers for compulsory treatment.

Opium Dens Within the Territory Must Close by a Deadline

The bureau has discovered that some unemployed people are privately running opium dens within the territory, providing opium for others to smoke, totaling no less than 2,000 establishments. At a time when opium prohibition is being strictly enforced, privately running opium dens is illegal. Considering their ignorance, police officers have been dispatched to advise them to close down by the end of this month. If any opium dens are discovered thereafter, the main offenders will be detained and handed over to the Garrison Headquarters for legal action. The landlords (or second landlords) will also be severely punished to achieve the goal of thorough elimination.

Extensive Publicity Urges Repentance

The Municipal Anti-Opium Committee and the Opium Addict Registration Section of the Public Security Bureau are conducting anti-opium work, starting with official propaganda to urge opium addicts to repent voluntarily. Therefore, in addition to sending staff from the Opium Addict Registration Section of the Public Security Bureau to conduct district-by-district propaganda, the Anti-Opium Committee is also using written propaganda, which has been quite effective. These two anti-opium agencies, realizing that the registration of opium addicts is about to end, are deeply concerned that some ignorant opium addicts are still waiting and seeing. Therefore, they have decided to jointly send staff to broadcast on various radio stations and screen anti-opium films within the next few days to urge opium addicts to repent and register as soon as possible during this period to avoid violating the law.

Punishment According to Military Law for Those Discovered After the Deadline

Our reporter interviewed Dai Lizhen, the director of the Opium Addict Registration Section of the Public Security Bureau, yesterday. According to him, the registration of opium addicts will end as scheduled at the end of this month and will not be extended. Starting on January 1st of next year, spot checks will be conducted on those who have quit opium to see if they still have opium addiction. Those found to still be addicted will be severely punished. As for opium addicts who are discovered without registration after the deadline, they will be detained and handed over to the Garrison Headquarters for legal action and will not be pardoned.

Ministry of Finance Instructs Banking Industry Yesterday to Accept Real Estate Mortgages According to Regulations; The Three Banks Are Instructed to Prepare for the Establishment of a Specialized Bank According to Regulations; and to Consult with the Central Bank to Expedite Rediscounting

The Ministry of Finance yesterday instructed the two associations of the banking industry, stating that, according to a report from the Shanghai Cotton Yarn Industry Association, the end of the year is approaching, and business is in danger. They respectfully request a review and implementation of the current temporary relief measures. The case found that on November 4th of this year, your ministry issued a public announcement designating the banknotes of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications as legal tender, stating, "The above measures are an essential plan for economic revival and are not intended to use finance as a goal. The organization of the Central Bank will also strive to improve to fulfill the functions of a bank. The general banking system must be reformed and sound, and under stable conditions, methods should be found to increase its liquidity so that it can supply the needs of legitimate industrial and commercial enterprises with sufficient funds. Real estate mortgage loan banks will be added, and real estate mortgage laws will be revised to revitalize real estate." Your ministry also recognizes that today's financial institutions are insufficient to save the declining market and allow it to recover. Therefore, it indicates that after the implementation of the new currency policy, a new economic policy will be implemented at the same time to remedy the situation. After hearing this order, the industrial and commercial sectors eagerly await its realization and express their grievances and want to express their humble opinions. Today, under the centralized reserve system, the funds for the issuance sector cannot be used due to centralization, and the funds for the operating sector cannot be recovered due to stagnant accounts. Therefore, the currency in the market has a tightening phenomenon, making it more difficult for industrial and commercial sectors to circulate. In addition, real estate remains stagnant. The hundreds of millions of credit chips used in the past are almost worthless. Recently, the credit chips launched, such as acceptance bills, cannot be fully accepted and discounted by the financial industry because the rediscounting system has not been implemented, and the power of bill circulation is still limited. Shanghai, known as the first city in the country, has hundreds of millions of old chips that are ineffective, and new chips have not been born. How can the industrial and commercial sectors not fall into a state of exhaustion? Therefore, they dare to jointly express the crisis and urge implementation, and publicly elect Wen Lanting, Lao Jingxiu, Gu Xinyi, Ma Jiliang, Jin Runxiang, Ke Ganchen, Zhu Wenqi, Luo Qinghua, Zhou Bangjun, etc., to submit petitions, respectfully requesting review and approval, and instructing them to handle it separately, which is convenient. In addition to the difficulties mentioned, your ministry has already considered them and has repeatedly ordered them to maintain them for a year, and each settlement period has been safely passed. The recent implementation of the legal tender policy is an essential plan for economic revival. Since its implementation, finance has gradually become more active, and the market has turned around. Your ministry is also actively drafting and revising various financial laws and regulations to improve the banking and financial system and facilitate the development of enterprises, and has sent a letter to the Central Bank to recruit commercial shares according to law and reorganize to fulfill the responsibilities of the bank. Real estate mortgage banks are also actively being prepared, and in order to activate land credit, a petition has been submitted to the Executive Yuan to transfer and discuss with the Legislative and Judicial Yuans to revise real estate mortgage laws and land and factory bases, which can facilitate mortgage loans. At the same time, it has also consulted with the Central Bank to expedite the rediscounting of bills to facilitate the circulation of funds, which is in line with the meaning of the association to activate old chips and circulate new chips. Those who request the transfer of land deeds for mortgages should be done as much as possible, which is inconsistent with the regulations of the Three Banks. It has been instructed to prepare for the establishment of a real estate mortgage loan bank by the deadline to meet the needs. As for the order to instruct all banks to accept mortgages of factory bases and factory properties, it has been transferred to the banking industry association to inform all banks. It is urgently ordered that the association be informed and that all members of the industry be notified that they should handle the requests for mortgages of factory bases and factory properties from manufacturers in accordance with the regulations, which is most important. This order.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, since the rent reduction movement occurred in this city, although some landlords have voluntarily reduced rents, they are still a minority. The rent reduction associations in various districts sent another letter to the Real Estate Association yesterday, warning them to consider the social market and the livelihood of the poor and to promptly order members to voluntarily reduce rents. The original letter and the progress of various parties are recorded below:

District Associations Warn Landlords

The rent reduction associations in various districts of the city sent a letter to the Real Estate Association yesterday, stating, "Dear Sirs, Shanghai has been affected by the economic downturn, all industries are in decline, prices have fallen sharply, and finance has lost its circulation, but rents remain high, making it difficult for the general public to bear this heavy burden. Therefore, they request that landlords in various places appropriately reduce rents to provide relief. We have organized a Rent Reduction Committee to reduce the burden on citizens and restore the market and save it from danger. We use righteous words to promote the awareness of landlords, so that they know the original intention of coexistence and common prosperity. In the past two years, although there have been landlords who are aware of the righteousness and consider the social environment and voluntarily or passively reduce rents, there are also many landlords who are blinded by profit and only know how to profit without knowing the overall situation. After careful investigation by our association, we have learned that the landlords who voluntarily reduce rents are all individual in nature and are not members of your association. Our association is suspicious of this. At this time, Shanghai, which has survived the disaster, is further affected by the economic tide of the world, resulting in the collapse of industry and commerce and the decline of the market. We should jointly come together to rescue the market. Your association should be aware of this. Now, the member landlords of your association not only do not know the overall situation and put the rescue of the market behind their minds, but even after repeated earnest requests from tenants, they still refuse to listen and even use economic power to enforce the law, disregarding human feelings, and often file lawsuits to oppress poor tenants, disregarding coexistence and common prosperity. This is truly a loss of reason due to greed and is regrettable. We believe that your association, as the leader of the real estate industry, should have the obligation to restrain member landlords to alleviate the people's difficulties. Now, rent reduction lawsuits are heard every day, and the poor are unbearable. In order to prevent unexpected events, the strong take risks, and the weak commit suicide. Your association disregards the social environment and allows member landlords to disobey public opinion. Our association hopes that your association will quickly realize this, consider the overall situation, and promptly order your members to voluntarily reduce rents, so as to reduce the burden on citizens and help restore the market. Then the tenants will be fortunate, and society will be fortunate."

A Gale Suddenly Occurred on the Sea; Both North and South Ocean Liners Were Affected; According to Reports from All Parties; Fortunately, No Danger Occurred

Since the night before last, the weather has been unusually cold, and the tide in the Huangpu River in Shanghai has also risen. The Sichuan Road and Guangdong Road area has been flooded with tide water from the sewers for several days. At the same time, a gale occurred on the sea, hindering merchant ships. The situation is described as follows:

Taishun

The China Merchants Bureau's Taishun ship loaded cargo and passengers on the night of November 30th and set sail for Yantai and Tianjin. On the 1st of this month, the ship went out of the Wusongkou, and at first there was nothing wrong. Then a gale occurred on the sea. The captain of the Taishun ship, considering the excessive wind and waves and the danger of navigation, chose a sheltered place near ShilanSland to anchor and stop navigation to wait for the weather to change. Yesterday, the captain telegraphed Shanghai to report that he would set sail as soon as the wind and waves subsided.

Haixiang

The Haixiang ship is sailing to Laoyao. The captain of the ship telegraphed Shanghai yesterday, saying that when the ship reached the sea area between 122 degrees 24 minutes east longitude and 32 degrees 32 minutes north latitude, there was a sudden gale on the sea, which was very fierce. Our ship still struggled forward, and the speed was greatly reduced. After a long battle, it telegraphed yesterday that it had escaped danger. At the same time, there were many ships that encountered the wind on the sea and anchored to avoid it.

Gongping

Another Gongping ship was sailing from Qingdao back to Shanghai and was scheduled to enter the port yesterday morning and load cargo today. The ship reported that when it reached the sea area of 123 degrees 29 minutes east longitude and 29 degrees 38 minutes north latitude, the gale came and struck. The gale was so strong and the range of the wind was so large that the Gongping ship had no time to stop and avoid it, so it sailed against the wind and went through the danger of turbulent waves. Yesterday afternoon, it telegraphed that it had escaped danger and was heading to Shanghai. There was also the Nanhua liner Haiyuan, which sailed from Shantou and also encountered a gale on the way. Many of the north-south ocean liners of Taikoo and Jardine encountered wind and waves on the sea route in the past two days, but they were all reported to be safe. Now the wind has blown elsewhere, and the ships can arrive in Shanghai one after another.

Vegetable Vendors on Kangti Road Temporarily Allowed to Set Up Stalls by the French Municipal Council; Seeking Relief Before the Construction of the Vegetable Market

The vegetable stalls on Kangti Road in the French Concession of this port have been banned by the French Concession authorities for several months and have not been restored. Because of the interruption of their livelihoods, the stallholders have repeatedly sent representatives to the party and government organs of this city and Mr. Lu Bohong, a Chinese director of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession, to petition and request negotiations for restoration. However, the French authorities are planning to build a vegetable market and are unable to allow stalls to be set up on Kangti Road. Therefore, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession sent a letter to the vegetable vendor representatives a few days ago, and the stallholders were extremely panicked. Yesterday, they sent representatives Zhou Wenxian and others to petition Mr. Lu, a Chinese director, again, requesting relief. The details are recorded as follows:

Petition Situation

Yesterday at around 10 am, the stallholders publicly elected representatives Zhou Wenxian, Yue Yigui, Zuo Henghe, etc., three people, carrying a petition to the Huashang Tram Company in Nanshi to petition Mr. Lu Bohong. Mr. Lu personally received them and received the petition and stated the difficult situation of the stallholders' lives and requested that the French authorities be negotiated for relief. Mr. Lu immediately telephoned the French Municipal Council and negotiated with Director Wei Zhiren. The council agreed to temporarily allow the establishment of stalls before the construction of the vegetable market to provide relief. The representatives of the stallholders were satisfied and left.

Petition

The petition submitted by the representatives of the stallholders, Wenxian, etc., yesterday is recorded as follows: Dear Sir, Regarding the case of the French Concession authorities banning stalls on Kangti Road, the stallholders have repeatedly petitioned you to uphold justice and asked you to negotiate. We are grateful for your approval and asked the French Municipal Council to find a way to handle it so as to maintain our livelihood. However, it has been several months, and there is still no news of restoring the stalls. The stallholders and their families have been in extreme panic due to the interruption of their livelihoods, and some have even gone on hunger strike and are waiting to die. The miserable situation is understood by you. Now it is the end of the year and the cold season, and the lives of the poor are even more difficult. The stallholders feel that a great disaster is imminent. If there is no hope of setting up stalls, they will all become starving corpses. At that time, it will affect society and be related to security, which will be serious and great. You are charitable and generous and are admired by the world. You will definitely grant relief to the poor vendors. Therefore, we publicly elect representatives to express our suffering and beg you to negotiate with the French Council again to temporarily allow the establishment of stalls on the road. As soon as the construction of the vegetable market is completed, we will move in to avoid starvation. We are impatiently awaiting your orders.

Siamese Study Abroad Group Arrives in Shanghai

The "Chinese Buddhist Siamese Study Abroad Group" organized by Chinese Buddhists Shi Biguan, Dengci, etc. in Beijing has been organized with the support of Xiao Focheng, Dai Jitao, Yu Youren, Huang Jingwan, Ding Fubao, Hu Shi, Ju Zheng, Mei Guangxi, Zhang Taiyan, Jiao Yitang, Xie Zhuchen, Tang Mande, Ye Yuhu, Qu Yingguang, Wang Yiting, and Master Taixu of the Chinese Buddhist Society, Master Yuanying of the Chinese Buddhist Association. The group now has Shi Biguan (a 34-year-old student from the Wuchang Buddhist Academy in Hubei), Shi Dengci (a 32-year-old student from the Minnan Buddhist Academy in Shandong), Shi Xingjiao (a 35-year-old student from the Guanjia Buddhist Academy in Hunan), and Shi Jueyuan (a 27-year-old student from the Guanjia Buddhist Academy in Anhui). The group leader is Biguan, and there are two other people participating. The group departed from Beijing for Shanghai yesterday and stayed at the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Buddhist Society in the Xuebao Temple on Dongyouheng Road, Hongkou. It is said that after the group visits various parties in Shanghai, it will transfer to Hong Kong to meet with Master Taixu and then buy a boat to Bangkok, Siam. It is said that the purpose of this trip is to study the "Pali" and "Sanskrit" Buddhist scriptures of that country for a period of five years, and to study the life of Bhikkhu's alms-begging etiquette. At the same time, it will introduce the meaning, spirit, and vegetarian life of Chinese Buddhist virtues, as well as the Mahayana Buddhism's active worldly self-benefit and altruistic teachings, to that country as much as possible, so that the Buddhist culture of China and Siam can complement each other.

Water Company Notice; Users Should Pay Attention to Protecting Water Meters; Winter is Coming, Take Precautions Early; Water Pipes Should Be Kept Warm to Avoid Freezing

The Shanghai Water Company of the Public Concession issued a notice yesterday to all users to pay attention to protecting water meters in order to keep water pipes warm and prevent freezing, as winter is approaching. The main points of the notice are recorded as follows: (1) If water pipes freeze, resulting in damage to the water pipes and subsequent leakage after melting, or loss to other objects for other reasons, the company will not be responsible. (2) The best way to avoid freezing is to close the indoor switches firmly when the weather is extremely cold or swimming, and open the faucets of the iced water pipes to empty the water in the water pipes. (3) There is usually no need to empty the hot water pipe equipment, but users should check the water tanks in the attics and other water pipes and try their best to keep them warm. (4) Water meters, such as those installed in exposed positions, and their upper and lower water pipes, should be kept warm with straw or other materials to avoid freezing. As for the water consumption due to freezing or any other reason, the water fee recorded by the water meter shall be paid in full. The company is very willing to help users protect water pipes and other equipment, but only to the extent that the water pipes are not affected.

Special District Rickshaw Industry Association Held an Emergency General Meeting Yesterday Demanding the Vehicle Committee Continue Registering Rickshaw Pullers and Appointed Representatives Including Yin Zhiling to Negotiate

The Rickshaw Industry Association of the Special District, due to the Vehicle Committee of the Public Works Department limiting the issuance of rickshaw licenses, resulting in an insufficient number of rickshaws for pullers and significant losses, convened a temporary emergency general meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce Auditorium in Tianhou Palace yesterday morning at 9:00 AM to seek the welfare of the industry. Over 1,200 people attended, including Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, Hou Shaoan, Liu Zhenqiu, and Jin Chunlin. Gu Songmao chaired the meeting, and after customary greetings, the chairman first reported the significance of convening the meeting, followed by discussions and resolutions on the following proposals: (1) Proposal to standardize rickshaw rental prices. Resolved: The Ministry of Finance has stipulated that one yuan of legal tender is equivalent to six double-cent subsidiary coins. Rickshaw rental prices will follow the Public Works Department's regulations of 85 cents per day, calculated according to the legal tender stipulated by the Ministry. (2) Proposal to request the Public Works Department's Vehicle Committee to maintain the original agreement and continue registering rickshaw pullers permanently. Resolved: Passed. (3) Proposal to request exemption from scrutiny for new rickshaws regarding slight variations in paint color, provided the dimensions meet the Vehicle Committee's regulations. Resolved: Passed. (4) Proposal to appoint representatives to be responsible for negotiating with the Vehicle Committee on the above matters. According to the first phase of the reclamation outline, the number of recruited reclaimers is limited to 200. After receiving the permits, the overseas Chinese hesitated and waited for a long time without going to the village. Their qualifications as reclaimers should be cancelled immediately. However, out of consideration for the overseas Chinese, an extension of one month is granted, until December 31 of this year. If they still fail to arrive beyond the deadline, it will be considered their own fault, and their reclaimer slots will be filled by others. As for the travel documents submitted by the overseas Chinese and the receipts and permits issued by the former Relief Committee, they must be returned within the deadline for collection. Once the deadline has passed, this Commission will not be able to keep them for the overseas Chinese for a long time. This notice is hereby issued."

Public Works Department Schedule to Cancel Chinese Language Allowance Totaling 250,000 Yuan Annually

Foreign employees of the Public Works Department, including Japanese and Indian staff of the Police Department, are given a monthly allowance for learning Chinese, ranging from several taels to dozens of taels. In addition, there are lump-sum bonuses for passing the Chinese language proficiency test. These two expenses are quite considerable, amounting to 250,000 yuan annually based on the current total amount. The police department accounts for two-thirds of the total. Recently, the authorities, in order to reduce expenses, have issued a notice to their subordinates, indicating their intention to cancel it. The lump-sum bonus for passing the exam will also be changed to prizes or medals in the future, and the level of the exam will be raised. Those with excellent results will be given prizes and medals, and it will not be enough to just pass. These measures will be gradually implemented among Japanese and Indian police officers. However, in view of the impact on the interests of lower-level employees, the implementation of the entire plan will be postponed for five years. In addition, long-term employees of the Public Works Department and the police department whose appointments were before 1931 have been entitled to child allowance. This allowance has also been decided to be cancelled at the end of this year. However, the above-mentioned Chinese language allowance does not conflict with the original regulations of the Public Works Department, which stipulate mandatory Chinese language learning, and will not be changed. Because in certain positions, the degree of proficiency in Chinese is an important criterion for promotion. It is reported that the above-mentioned proposal for change was first drafted by the Director of the Finance Department of the Public Works Department, submitted to the Personnel Committee for review, and then submitted to the Board of Directors for approval and implementation.

After the Death of Female Professor Zhang Duanzhen, the Estate Dispute Has Not Ended. She Suffered Unfair Treatment During Her Lifetime. Wang Wenyu Knows the Most Details.

Zhang Duanzhen, a woman from Minhou, was well-versed in both Chinese and Western learning and had served as a professor at various universities. Unfortunately, she died of illness on July 26 of this year. During her lifetime, she strived to encourage herself, studied tirelessly, and accumulated assets of more than 10,000 yuan. On her deathbed, because she had many sisters, she made a will in advance, stating that in case of any misfortune, all her estate would be managed entirely by her brother, Zhang Xifan. The defendants, Zhang Meizhen and others, hired lawyer Suan Yaoxian to file a defense. After receiving the report, the court held several hearings and considered it necessary to summon witnesses. The plaintiffs and defendants, each accompanied by a lawyer, arrived in court one after another. Chief Judge Pang briefly questioned both parties. The defendant's lawyer stated that the defendant, in addition to the defense, also filed a counterclaim, alleging that the plaintiff forged the will and should be deprived of the right to inherit the estate according to law. According to the testimony of the witness, Ms. Lin Chen Shuduan, 47 years old, from Fuzhou, who is a relative of both the plaintiff and the defendant and was also a classmate, when asked whether Zhang Duanzhen made a will before her death, she replied, "Yes, and there were four of us present." Then the plaintiff's lawyer stated that the defendant, Zhang Meizhen, had recently written a letter to Ms. Wang Wenyu and the witness Lin Chen Shuduan, who is present in court, and asked the court to question them. Chief Judge Pang questioned Lin Chen Shuduan accordingly. She replied, "Zhang Meizhen wrote a letter to me, instructing me on how to testify in court and asked me to sign. I didn't think it was right and refused to sign. So this original letter was returned by my cousin Chen." At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that Ms. Wang Wenyu is currently a teacher at Jinghai Women's School in Suzhou and knows the details of how Zhang Duanzhen was driven out and treated by the defendants during her lifetime. Zhang Xifan submitted a notebook written by Bao Guobiao as supporting evidence for the will, which contained all the facts of Zhang Duanzhen's life. Chief Judge Pang examined it and ordered Bao Guoliang to testify in court. He said that he was from Zhejiang and the defendants were his wife's aunts. His wife's father was the defendants' brother. The notes he wrote were records of the deceased's oral accounts and were responsible proof. He said, "I am here today to speak the truth. I may offend my aunts." Chief Judge Pang then ordered Wang Wenyu and others to be summoned to court for further trial. Then the court adjourned.

Ministry of Finance Stipulates Measures for Investigating Violations of Stamp Tax in Other Provinces, to be Handled Separately by the Competent Authorities of Those Provinces

The personnel sent by the Ministry of Finance to supervise and inspect stamp tax in various provinces and cities have already begun their work separately. It has been learned that when performing their duties, the inspectors often discover cases of violations of the stamp tax law in other provinces or counties, so they have presented petitions to the Ministry asking how to handle them. The Ministry of Finance has now stipulated two measures: (1) When performing their duties, the inspectors discover cases of violations of the stamp tax law in other provinces or counties, they should submit them to the original competent authorities for investigation, and submit them to the provincial stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax bureau, or the finance office that also handles stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol, for verification and transfer to the judicial organs in the location of the store that violated the stamp tax law for trial in accordance with the law. (2) When performing their duties, the inspectors discover cases of violations of the stamp tax law in other provinces or counties, they should immediately send them by letter to the provincial stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax bureau, or the finance office that also handles stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol, for verification and transfer to the judicial organs in the location of the store that violated the stamp tax law for investigation in accordance with the law. It has been instructed to all provinces and cities to comply with it yesterday.

Austrian Professor Lectures on the Mysteries of Chinese Characters

Central News Agency reports: Yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM, at the International Theatre Association on the fourth floor of the Young Women's Christian Association at No. 55 Yuanmingyuan Road, the "Old Shanghai Exhibition," which began on the 26th of last month, invited Austrian national Mr. Leifler (Chinese name Luo Yimin) to lecture on "The Mysteries of Chinese Characters." Mr. Luo, aged 33, holds a PhD in Political Economy from the University of Vienna in Austria. Sixteen years ago, while at the University of Vienna, he studied Chinese with Luo Shide, a former Austrian envoy to China. He came to China in 1932 and is currently a German professor at Wentong University. Mr. Luo speaks fluent Chinese and is proficient in Chinese writing. He said that studying Chinese is not a difficult task. Although the Kangxi Dictionary contains more than 40,000 characters, only 3,000 to 4,000 characters are actually used. He then listed several characters such as "river" (河), "jiang" (江), and "brush" (筆) on the blackboard and explained their origins and meanings in detail, giving a lecture that lasted for more than an hour. Most of the attendees were female members of the association, about 50 people in total, and they were all very interested. It is said that a Westerner will be hosting a "fortune-telling session" on the afternoon of the 5th (the day after tomorrow) at 6:00 PM.

Rickshaw Owners Overcharging Fares: Reasons for Committee Penalties

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Rickshaw Affairs Committee, in view of the numerous cases of rickshaw owners overcharging fares, has had no choice but to take measures to stop this practice. Therefore, any rickshaw owner or contractor who violates the license regulations and overcharges fares will be subject to suspension of license issuance upon verification. Some of the rickshaw owners petitioned the trade association, which then sent a letter to the Rickshaw Affairs Committee days ago, requesting that it withdraw its order and be lenient, alleging that the Committee had listened to inaccurate reports from a few rickshaw pullers and arbitrarily punished the owners. The Chairman of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee issued a statement yesterday regarding this matter, strongly refuting the accusation that the Committee arbitrarily punishes without thorough investigation. He said that the Committee makes every effort to investigate after receiving a report, and before taking action, gives the rickshaw owner the opportunity to hear the evidence presented by the puller. In most cases, the contractor also admits to the offense. Therefore, the Committee never arbitrarily punishes rickshaw owners without solid evidence. Furthermore, the Committee believes that it is regrettable that some rickshaw owners have no sense of responsibility to abide by the conditions of license issuance. Although there are some sensible rickshaw owners who have done their best to advise their contractors to make every effort to maintain order, the Committee, in view of the limited effectiveness of their advice, feels that it has no choice but to exercise its disciplinary powers. However, the Committee believes that the financial burden of being penalized should be borne by those rickshaw owners who violate the regulations. The purpose of the penalties is to prevent overcharging of fares. Therefore, it hopes that people in the rickshaw trade association can consider the hardships of the rickshaw pullers and sincerely cooperate in this matter. In addition, the Hongkou Rickshaw Puller Licensing Office has now closed. From now on, all matters will be handled by the New Zhapu/Shunde Road Public Works Department district licensing office. Furthermore, owners of private rickshaws whose pullers' licenses expired at the end of September are also requested to have their pullers renew their licenses as soon as possible, as new regulations will soon be enforced, and anyone without a current arm badge will not be allowed to operate.

Leave for Examinations Considered Official Business: Explanation to be Provided to Concession Authorities by Ministry

Tang Mengjun, a teacher at the Shanghai Municipal Council's Middle School, was previously approved to register for the higher examinations after passing the qualification review by the Higher Examination Qualification Review Committee. However, due to not being granted leave, he was unable to take the examination. This situation was reported to the authorities. Yesterday, the Higher Examination First Examination Affairs Office issued approval letter No. 15, noting that civil servants and teachers who apply for leave to take examinations may be granted leave as official business, which has long been ordered by the National Government to be followed and has been established as a precedent. Regarding the previous situation, it is requested that a letter be sent to the Examination Yuan, which will then forward it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, instructing the office to explain the significance of the higher examinations to the concession authorities to avoid any impact.

Li Zhentai Arrested for Smoking Opium: Fellow Villager Takes Advantage to Defraud, Sends Letter to Father-in-Law Claiming Arrest for Theft, 500 Yuan Remittance Embezzled

Li Zhenqin, a Shandong native, 52 years old, residing at No. 44, Nanyongjili, Wangzhi Road, French Concession, who runs a pharmacy, was arrested on August 16th for smoking opium, handed over to the court for prosecution, and sentenced to a fine of 20 yuan and one month of mandatory detoxification. However, Li Benzheng, a fellow villager, 40 years old, who previously resided upstairs at the Shanji Barber Shop, No. 140 Beidili Road, French Concession, and now resides at No. 2, Zhenqingli, New Guangdong Street, Chuan Highway, Hongkou, falsely used the name of Li Zhenqin's wife, née Li Yuan, and sent a letter to Yuan Guoshan, Li Zhentai's father-in-law in Shandong, stating that his son-in-law had been detained in Shanghai for theft and needed 500 yuan to be sent abroad in order to find a way to avoid punishment, that he was unable to raise the money in Shanghai, and therefore wrote to borrow the money immediately. Upon receiving the letter, Yuan Guoshan, knowing that something had happened to his son-in-law in Shanghai and concerned about family ties, immediately gathered the full amount of 500 yuan and entrusted the Shandong Zhuqiao Telegraph Bureau to remit it to the Tianhexing Remittance Agency on Tiantang Street, Aiduya Road, French Concession, Shanghai. After receiving the reply telegram from Yuan Guoshan of Shandong, Li Benzheng immediately carved a seal in the name of Li Zhentai and, with the guarantor of the owner of the Shanji Barber Shop at No. 140 Beidili Road, where he originally resided, fraudulently withdrew the money from the Tianhexing Remittance Agency and embezzled it. Later, after Li Zhentai completed his one-month opium detoxification period, paid the fine, and was released from prison, he returned home and immediately went to his hometown in Shandong to meet his father-in-law, Yuan Guoshan, and learned that someone had taken the opportunity to impersonate him and commit fraud. He immediately came to Shanghai, investigated the person who withdrew the money from Tianhexing Remittance Agency, and learned that it was guaranteed by the Shanji Barber Shop, knowing that it was Li Benzheng who had done it. When he went to look for Li Benzheng, he had already moved away. He immediately reported the information to the French Police and requested an arrest. Detective Li Liansheng and Bao Detective Yu Wenzhi investigated and learned that Li Benzheng had moved to No. 2, Zhenqingli, Chuan Highway. They went to arrest him together with the local police, but Li was not at home. On the 30th of last month at noon, Li Benzheng happened to be passing by Beiler Road in the French Concession, and was encountered by Detective Li and Detective Yu, who immediately arrested him and took him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was handed over to the Criminal Division 1 of the Special District 2 Court, presided over by Judge Zhang Chaozuo. Attorney Fei Xizhen of the Police Department stated the case, stating that the defendant was arrested for forging documents and committing fraud, that the Police Department's investigation was incomplete, and that a fugitive accomplice needed to be arrested. He requested a postponement and that the defendant be detained temporarily pending a detailed investigation of the case and a request for a hearing. The court verified the report and questioned the defendant Li Benzheng, who admitted that he had written the letter in the name of another person and committed fraud. The court ordered a rehearing on the 6th and the defendant was returned to custody.
