Dancer Huang Aizhen Sues for Indecent Assault: No Withdrawal of Charges Allowed, Trial Concluded Yesterday

Huang Aizhen, a dancer from Huzhou at the New York Dance Hall, previously had her father, Huang Wenkui, as her legal representative, retain a lawyer to sue Jiang Bifeng, a shareholder of the Xiaoyao Dance Hall, in the First Special District Court for indecent assault. The case had been heard twice. Because the two parties had reached a settlement outside of court, the attorney representing the plaintiff requested to withdraw the charges. However, Judge Jiang Shuzi, presiding over the case, ruled that withdrawal was not permitted because the alleged violation of Article 240 of the Criminal Code, as claimed by the plaintiff, was not subject to settlement, and rescheduled the hearing. Details were previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the continuation of the hearing. Both the plaintiff and the defendant were present in court awaiting instructions. The plaintiff, Huang Wenkui, claimed to be a 47-year-old native of Huzhou, currently residing at the home of a relative at No. 4, Yikangli, Xinkai Road, and that Aizhen was his 16-year-old daughter who had been betrothed to someone in her hometown but had not yet married. He was suing the defendant for seducing his daughter, but that the details needed to be asked of Aizhen. Furthermore, as the case had already been settled, he did not wish to pursue the matter further. Huang Aizhen then claimed to be 16 years old, born in December, initially claiming to be a "sheep" (肖羊) and then a "monkey" (肖猴). She began working as a dance partner at the Xiaoyao Dance Hall on July 1st of this year. She subsequently had a relationship with the defendant and rented a house together at No. 10, Chengqili, Race Course Road. They had now written a document severing the cohabitation relationship. The defendant, Jiang Bifeng, claimed that the plaintiff Huang Aizhen was already 21 years old and previously cohabitated with her lover, Zhou Ziyu, at No. 50, Xiangfen Lane. When she joined the Xiaoyao Dance Hall in July of this year, Huang also claimed to be 21 years old. As he was a shareholder of the dance hall, he became acquainted with Huang. On the night of August 17th, Huang was arguing with her lover at the entrance of the dance hall and they went to the Chengdu Road Police Station together, where she also reported that she was 21 years old. These facts could be investigated. Later, Huang Aizhen fell ill and did not have the money for medical treatment, so he provided it. After recovering, she voluntarily cohabitated with him and sent a letter to her father, Huang Wenkui, who replied and permitted it. Therefore, on September 18th, he signed a cohabitation agreement with Huang, with lawyer Cao Lin as the witness. The agreement stated that Huang Jinbao (Aizhen) was 21 years old. He submitted the agreement to the court. Huang Aizhen also stated that when she was a dancer at Xiaoyao, she claimed to be 21 years old because according to the dance hall's regulations, those under 16 were not allowed to dance. After Judge Jiang verified the statements, he made the following pronouncement: "Today, this court received an anonymous letter stating that the plaintiff and his daughter colluded to extort the defendant, and that the name Huang Wenkui is false and that there is actually no such person." He then asked Huang whether the person present today was her father named Huang Wenkui, and the woman replied that he was indeed her father Huang Wenkui. Judge Jiang then questioned the defendant Jiang Bifeng whether he had written the letter, to which Jiang replied that he did not know. After arguments by the defendant's lawyer, Zhou Yongding, the court ordered the case to be continued and the verdict to be announced next Monday. Jiang Bifeng paid a bail of 500 yuan.

Attention of Russian Émigrés: Murder Case – More Than One Hundred Spectators – The Murderer's Account of the Incident

The forty-eight-year-old Russian, Botkilian (transliteration), the owner of a Russian bakery and confectionery shop at No. 234-6 Avenue Albert, French Concession, became enraged because his employed fellow countryman, Semianov, thirty years old, had committed an indecent act against Botkilian's seven-year-old daughter. The deceased suffered ten stab wounds all over his body. Afterward, Botkilian surrendered himself to the French police station. The police detained him and transported the body to the coroner's office, requesting the Special No. 2 Court to send personnel to examine it. Botkilian was then sent to the Special No. 2 Court for interrogation and preliminary investigation. All these details have been reported in this newspaper. The case was concluded by the French Police Department, and the defendant was brought before the Special No. 2 Court for further interrogation yesterday afternoon. More than a hundred Russians, men, women, and children, attended the court hearing. At 11:00 AM, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the hearing in the First Criminal Court. Attorney Fei Xizhen of the Police Department presented the case, charging the defendant with murder under Article 271 of the Criminal Code. Subsequently, the Western detective in charge of the case from the Police Department reported on the investigation process. The defendant was interpreted by Zhang Qingchun, the Russian translator of the High Court. According to the translated testimony, the deceased committed an indecent act against Botkilian's daughter. When Botkilian questioned the deceased, he became threatening, so Botkilian grabbed a sharp knife, intending only to scare him. However, the deceased forcefully seized the knife from his hand, resulting in an injury to his own throat, which led to his death. The defense lawyers, including Premier Lawyer, were hired to defend him. The court also summoned the defendant's wife and daughter for questioning. The court then adjourned, scheduling a later date for further proceedings. The defendant remains in custody.

Near-Fatal Coal Gas Poisoning

Wang Agou, a twenty-seven-year-old local resident with no house number on Huangxing Road, Changluo Township, Eastern Shanghai, married a woman from Songjiang two years ago. Over the years, the couple has faced difficulties in their daily lives. Agou spends his days peddling vegetables, sometimes also working as a small vendor. His hard-earned income is barely enough to make ends meet. His wife, nearing her full term of pregnancy, suddenly experienced abdominal pain around 11:00 PM last night, indicating that she was about to give birth. They called in midwife Madam Lu to assist with the delivery and burned coal for warmth. After the birth, the fire was left unextinguished. Unfortunately, the house was small and lacked windows for ventilation. Around 2:00 AM, Agou returned home after shopping and suddenly saw his wife lying stiffly in bed and the baby suffocated and silent. He cried out for help, and neighbors rushed to the scene, unsure of what to do. Fortunately, someone was quick-witted enough to call the Hongkou Civilian Maternity Hospital via telephone. A doctor rushed to the scene by car. He quickly sensed the coal gas, which was suffocatingly unbearable, and diagnosed coal gas poisoning. The mother's spleen and uterus were also affected. He performed surgery and fortunately caught it early enough to prevent death. However, the baby was already bluish-purple and could not be saved.

The Effective Medicine for High Blood Pressure, Rest-Quell Spirit – High blood pressure is the cause of stroke, and there has never been a good treatment. Since British doctors invented the effective medicine for high blood pressure, "Rest-Quell Spirit," it has been highly valued by the medical community in various countries. Articles on the results of "Rest-Quell Spirit" in medical journals have been continuously published. The first users of this medicine in our country were hospitals in various church groups. Four years ago, when the Chinese Medical Association held a national conference, members presented articles on Rest-Quell Spirit. However, this medicine had no distribution point in China and had to be ordered from the United States, which was very inconvenient. Since the beginning of the year, the American pharmaceutical factory has entrusted the Zhongxi Pharmacy on Four Horses Road in Shanghai as the general manager for China, making it convenient for buyers. Initially, due to the price of gold, the selling price was quite high. When the price of gold was lowest this summer, the pharmacy re-ordered a new price, greatly reducing it. Recently, the price of gold has risen again, and the price of many imported goods has risen again. However, the pharmacy has sufficient stock of Rest-Quell Spirit and does not raise prices. Sports News

Czech Davis Cup Player Meng Ruier Performed in Shanghai Yesterday – Wonderful Shots in Succession, Worthy of a First-Class Player – Performing Two Singles and Doubles Matches, Departing for Hong Kong Today

Czechoslovakian Davis Cup representatives Meng Ruier and Haixu, who were performing in Japan, passed through Shanghai yesterday on their way back to Europe. They arrived here on the Japanese ship Qingguo Maru. The Shanghai Chinese Tennis Club specially invited Meng and Haixu to perform, with Carson and Defu as their partners, performing one singles and one doubles match each. Many Chinese and Western tennis fans went to watch, about a thousand people, mostly Westerners. The weather was cold, but there was such a grand occasion, which shows their appeal. The singles and doubles were won by the Czech players. The wonderful parts were met with continuous applause. Mr. Meng left Shanghai this morning for Hong Kong, or may visit India, it is said.

Skill

Mr. Meng is the seventh-ranked male singles player in the world on grass courts. Last year, in Wimbledon, he reached the last eight in singles. Yesterday's performance showed wonderful skills in succession, worthy of a famous player. He defeated Carson in straight sets, without fully displaying his strengths. The most noticeable thing was his extraordinary quickness, with a powerful high-pressure, much better than Xu Chengji. His backhand accuracy is unparalleled, and he mostly wins with his backhand. His forehand is rather average. He often goes to the net, and his volleys and half-volleys in front of the net are also his strengths. Wei Xun's performance also had many wonderful shots, but unfortunately, in front of a famous player, his courage was too small. Later, he discovered Meng's weakness and repeatedly attacked Meng's forehand, scoring many points. Haixu is younger and has refined tennis skills. Although he has no special points, he is capable in all aspects and refined. He has a promising future. The doubles performance of the two is not as good as their singles. Their cooperation is not yet in a good state. In the first set, Card was very likely to win, but unfortunately, Defu often made mistakes, often making mistakes at important moments, so there was not much excitement.

From right to left: Defu, Carson, Haixu, Meng Ruier (Photo by Zhu Shunlin)

Singles

The singles match was Meng Ruier vs. Carson. Meng Ruier served first, extremely sharp. Carson was unable to cope with the left and right blocks, and was defeated in a single set. Carson tried to cheer up, using long shots from the baseline, Meng slightly negligent, and each scored one point. After that, Meng sailed smoothly, with long shots far away, the ball deep into the sidelines, and sometimes he went to the net to block, or lightly or obliquely or pressed or picked, and although Carson had a good performance, but it was difficult to succeed, and there were many errors, so he lost the first set with a score of 1 to 6. Meng took advantage of the winning streak, using his refined tennis skills, using his racket, with powerful cuts, and winning three consecutive sets. By the fourth set, Carson displayed his strengths, winning after several ties. Although Meng's serve was fast, it lacked accuracy, and his high-ball smash was unique. Carson relied on his long shots and took advantage of Meng's weakness and fatigue, winning two more sets, but in the end he was defeated by his inferior skills. Meng also won the second set with a score of 6 to 3. In the third set, Carson served first. Carson worked hard to fight, with good performances, winning the second set after fierce competition, but the strength was disparate, and he finally lost with a score of 6 to 1.

Doubles

The doubles match was held after the singles, Meng Ruier, Haixu vs. Carson, Defu. At the beginning of the battle, the line-up of both sides was quite loose. Meng Ruier was tall, Haixu was short, and the cooperation was not good. Carson and Defu were also as expected, with more errors. The Czech team first won two sets, and then lost one set by suicide. After that, there were errors on both sides from time to time, and the Shanghai team chased to four to four. The Czech team relied on Meng to win. Back and forth, and equal again, and finally Meng's skills were superior, and the Czech team won the first set with a score of nine to seven. After this, the Czech team still dominated. Defu Carson made mistakes in succession, and the offense and defense were not appropriate. Meng's serve was like a cannonball, and Haixu gradually got into the groove, handy. They won the second set with a score of 6 to 2. In the third set, Carson took the lead in serving, winning one set, and then pressed hard. Meng and Hai were very negligent, and Shanghai won the last set with a score of 6 to 2. The performance of the two sides gradually improved, the situation was tense, the score was quite close, and Meng still won with a score of 6 to 4.

Jinan Wins Over Youyou

Education News

Recent Situation of Colleges and Universities in Peiping and Tientsin: Education Association Decides to Lead Students to Petition the Authorities; Presidents Bai and Xu of Peida Negotiating with the Ministry of Education in Nanking

(Special dispatch from Peiping) The national colleges and universities and private universities in Peiping and Tientsin are extremely concerned about the current situation. The presidents of the four universities, Jiang Menglin, Xu Boming, Mei Yi Qi, and Li Zheng, as well as professors Hu Shi and Jiang Tingfu, visited Song Zheyuan, the garrison commander of Peiping and Tianjin, twice to inquire about the truth.

The Joint Association of Faculty and Staff of National Colleges and Universities in Peiping and Tientsin held a meeting at the Zhongnan East Fourth Office at 10 AM today (the 1st). Committee members Li Xiaoyan, Xu Zhi, Ma Zhidao, Wang Yongquan, Mu Mo, Wang Jixu, Jia Chengzhang, Cai Zengtang, and Yang Likui attended. The chairman first reported on the progress of past association affairs and the work to be carried out in the future, and then reported in detail on the recent situation in North China. After the meeting, the committee members went to the Shuai Fu Yuan Yi Yuan in Dongcheng for a dinner. During the dinner, Yang Likui and Xu Zhi were designated as representatives to contact the authorities of National Peking University, Peiping University, Normal University, and Tsinghua University separately in the next two days, and all faculty, staff, and students will participate in the work. The Education Association representatives plan to petition Song Zheyuan soon and send a telegram regarding the current situation. According to a committee member, given the situation in the North, the central government should make stabilizing people's hearts one of its main tasks. However, the funding for the colleges and universities has not yet been remitted. The Peiping-Tientsin Higher Education Funding Management Committee sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Education today (the 1st) to urge the payment of the funds, as the arrival of the education funds in Peiping would also help stabilize the hearts of the education community. The text of the telegram urging the payment of funds is recorded below: Nanjing Ministry of Finance: The November education funds have not yet been remitted. The colleges and universities are in urgent need of funds. Please remit the funds to Peiping as soon as possible so that they can be disbursed. Peiping-Tientsin Higher Education Funding Management Committee.

Since Bai Pengfei, the dean of the College of Law and Commerce of National Peiping University, and Xu Shoushang, the dean of the Women's College of Arts and Sciences, went to Nanking, the students in each college have been attending classes well. According to professors, rumors of the relocation of Peiping University colleges to the south are not true, considering the overall situation of Peiping University. The students are currently attending classes in compliance with the Ministry of Education's order not to slack off. When Presidents Bai and Xu return to Peiping, there will be a concrete plan. On the day before Presidents Bai and Xu went to Nanking, the professors of each college initiated a professors' meeting, which resulted in two points: (1) Presidents Bai and Xu, representing the entire Peiping University, should go to Nanking to express the sincere attitude of Peking University and ask the Ministry of Education for instructions on all matters. (2) The Peiping University Professors' Conference will publish a letter to the students, praising the drafter. The content of the letter will make an overall and accurate statement to the students. However, whether this letter to the students will be issued will be decided after Presidents Bai and Xu return to Peiping.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Boy

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

This made Robert completely convinced, so Nancy led him through the shallow waters, over dangerous rocks, and he followed blindly. After many detours, she led him to a small cave in a large rock, where the scorched stones clearly showed that someone had made a fire there before.

"Isn't this interesting?" Nancy asked, taking a little bread mixed with oil from her bag. However, it no longer resembled a machine because it was mixed with nails, fishhooks, stones, and other debris.

"Yes, but do you think they won't find us?" Robert asked, feeling that the secluded mountain ravine was boring and starting to think about his other companions.

"No, I don't, because if I hear them coming, I'll hide and watch how they look for me. That would be fun."

"They might not come anymore."

"I don't care. I can go back myself."

"Isn't it very far?" Robert asked, looking at his small, rough boots, which were thirsty and covered in scratches after the long journey.

"I think it's about six miles." Nancy's concept of distance was vague, but she was very confident in her abilities.

"I think we should go back now," Robert suggested again soon after.

"I'm not going yet, I want to pick more blackberries," Nancy said, and started picking them. Robert was getting impatient.

Suddenly, the sun went behind the mountain, and he sighed, "You said you would take good care of me."

"I am taking care of you, and doing my best. Don't be fussy, little boy. I'll go in a while." Nancy said, thinking that a six-year-old Robert was just a baby compared to her.

So little Robert sat still, looking around with a worried heart, but he waited patiently, because although he was quite apprehensive, he found Nancy to be very trustworthy.

"I think it will be night soon," he muttered to himself, just as a mosquito bit him and the frogs in the nearby pond began to play their twilight ensemble.

We hereby reply to you, hoping for your understanding. Shang Zhen."

Shanghai Middle School Teacher Training Research Association's Examination Group Held Second Meeting Yesterday: Discussed Graduation Examinations and Grade Evaluation

The Graduation Examination Group of the Shanghai Middle School Teacher Training Research Association held its second meeting at the Huzhou Society on Guizhou Road at 4 PM yesterday. Attendees included Chen Jicheng, Tao Guangchuan, Wang Yukai, Zhang Jiashu, Xu Renhan, Tang Naikang, Yang Daohong, Lu Shiyin, Ruan Zongxian, Li Haopei, Chen Mengyu, Gu Jiwu, Cao Yanshen, Feng Yixian, and Tao Zailiang. Chen Jicheng was the chairman, and Tao Guangchuan was the recorder. The issues discussed were: (1) Whether graduation examinations should be abolished. The results were: (A) The intention of the examination system is good, but there are many malpractices. In theory, it should be abolished. (B) Before it is abolished, methods of remediation should be sought quickly. (C) Remediation methods are as follows: (a) The examination should be based on students, not schools, and the examination results should not be ranked by school. (b) Improve the examination questions and scoring methods. (2) How to change the examination scoring method. The result was to use the examination score as the standard. (3) How many minor tests should be held per semester? The result was to use the number of class hours per week as the standard. (4) The advantages and disadvantages of using test-style and problem-style methods to examine student grades. The result was to use the nature of the subject as the standard and let the teachers use their discretion in choosing the method. (5) What scoring method is most suitable for recording grades? It was decided to discuss this at the next meeting. (6) How should a student who fails one or two subjects in the examination and still fails after a makeup exam be helped? The result was to follow the regulations of the Ministry of Education.

Private School Association Requests Public Concession to Increase Subsidies: Appoints Feng Yixian and Others as Representatives to Request from the Taxpayers' Association, and Opposes Considering School Telephones as Business Telephones

The Shanghai Public Concession Private School Association held a general meeting and dinner party at the Daguanlou on Simalu at 6 PM yesterday. Attendees included Chen Jicheng, Cui Jianwu, Xu Renhan, Sun Yucai, Feng Yixian, Qian Shenzhi, Zhang Lingfei, Zhu Shaoping, Guo Shouchun, Weng Guoxun, Jin Guozhang, Yu Shenzhai, and Xuan Bokun, representatives from Shangzhong, Daozhong, Minzhi, Shangxiao, Minguo, Huanian, Shanggong, Binhai, Zhende, Tongshan, Minfu, Huanqiu, Pin'er, Qunyi, Peiming, YMCA, Suzhou, Yizhao, Ziqiang, Zhenyi, and other schools, totaling more than eighty people. Chen Jicheng was the chairman, and Sun Yucai was the recorder. The resolutions were: (1) To request the Public Concession Bureau to increase subsidies. Feng Yixian, Cui Jianwu, Jin Tongzhang, Xu Renhan, and Qian Shenzhi were appointed as representatives to carry an official letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association. Sun Yucai will draft the official letter, and Xu Renhan and Cui Jianwu will contribute ideas. (2) The case of reducing private school rental fees will be handed over to the executive committee for detailed discussion and decision. (3) The Public Concession Telephone Company considers school telephones as business telephones and should be argued against on the basis of reason. (4) According to reports from the majority of members, some people are selling various school supplies in the name of the association. Those who have been deceived can submit a written request to the association for assistance. The meeting then adjourned, and the Hujiang Bookstore Company in the Junyi Lane of the Concession distributed a copy of the Graphic Calligraphy Textbook to each person.

Ye Xin'an Gave a Lecture at the China Women's Physical Education Teachers' School Yesterday

The China Women's Physical Education Teachers' School on Connaught Road invited Mr. Ye Xin'an to give a lecture at the school at 9 AM yesterday. The topic was "The North China Problem for Two Thousand Years." Mr. Ye gave a simple explanation of the current situation in North China and international relations, and then traced the situation in North China through the Zhou, Qin, Han, Jin, Tang, Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. He gave a detailed explanation of the causes and effects of the current crisis in North China, citing historical evidence and interweaving stories with humor, which captivated the audience. The lecture lasted for an hour before ending.

Women's Education Center to Hold Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition on the 8th

The Shanghai Women's Education Center will hold a one-week calligraphy and painting exhibition at the center from the 8th to the 15th of this month to promote women's art, encourage artists, and provide opportunities for the general public to appreciate and study art. The exhibits will be divided into: (1) Calligraphy, including famous people's handwriting, couplets, central scrolls, horizontal scrolls, and screen strips, regardless of whether the calligraphy is in regular, clerical, seal, or any other style; (2) Traditional Chinese painting, including ancient and modern famous paintings and original works, regardless of whether they are landscapes, flowers, figures, birds, or animals; (3) Western painting, including oil paintings, pastels, charcoal drawings, cartoons, watercolors, patterns, and advertising paintings. It is said that the center is now accepting submissions, and applicants should submit their works to the center before the 5th. If submitting from outside the city by mail, it must be registered. The center will be responsible for the safekeeping of the exhibits during the exhibition period. Artists who wish to sell their works should indicate the price. If a work is sold, the center will deduct 20% to cover the exhibition costs.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— by Zhou Shoujuan

In the past, when the state of Yue was destroyed by the state of Wu, King Goujian of Yue and his queen were also taken prisoner. King Fucha of Wu ordered him to crawl and acknowledge his submission, so he crawled and acknowledged his submission. He was imprisoned in a stone chamber, so he was imprisoned in a stone chamber. He was even forced to taste excrement, so he tasted excrement, and he was ordered to raise horses, so he raised horses, humbly enduring all kinds of humiliation. It can truly be said that he showed great patience. However, later, with the help of Bo Pi, he was released back to his country. He endured hardship and bitterness, sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall, diligently working in obscurity for ten years to build up resources and ten years to educate the people. In addition, Fan Li and Xi Shi, for the sake of their country, were determined to sacrifice themselves. Finally, he avenged himself, wiped out the humiliation, and destroyed the state of Wu. This ancient story is a very good lesson and a very good example for us. Everyone should keep it in mind and worship King Goujian of Yue as an idol. Recently, I watched the Shanghai Theater's performance of "Xi Shi" in Suzhou, which greatly excited me. The performers, such as Ms. Cheng Jingzi as Xi Shi, Ms. Xu Lilin as Zheng Dan, Lu Pingjun as Fucha, Fan Yinpu as Goujian, Qian Feng as Fan Li, Xing Jinhu as Wu Zixu, and Bai Xiongfei as Bo Pi, all worked very hard, giving us a very deep impression. This makes me even more admire the directing skills of Chen Dabei and Gu Wenzong. After the performance in Suzhou, I heard that they will also perform in Wuxi and Changshu, which is truly a meritorious deed. Lovable artists! I offer you a pinch of incense, wishing you well for the country. Travel thousands of miles, perform thousands of times, to awaken those compatriots who are living in a drunken dream. Having already played the first half of Goujian, don't forget to play the second half of Goujian!

Hidden Silver

— Yan

Amidst the clamor to abolish silver, two stories of hidden silver, long buried in the depths of my mind, were stirred up.

In my hometown, there was a large farming household, led by an old man with five strong sons and three hired laborers, cultivating over a hundred mu of land. The entire family, young and old, worked diligently, and were unusually frugal, accumulating significant savings each year. Although outwardly they appeared no different from anyone else, those within dozens of miles suspected them to be immensely wealthy. The old man had no love for paper money, only for white silver. He also distrusted banks, so he secretly buried his silver at home, concealing its location even from his five daughters-in-law. One moonlit night three years ago, dozens of armed bandits broke into the household. The family scattered, but the old man was captured. The bandits demanded he reveal the location of the hidden silver, but he refused to hand over his family's hard-earned wealth. The bandits then subjected him to torture, from binding and beating to pouring water over his head and burning his genitals, but he remained steadfastly silent. At this time, two of his daughters-in-law, hiding on the roof ridge, watched the horrific torture of their father-in-law in the rear house. They cried out, urging him to reveal the silver's location. The old man, unable to endure any longer, finally relented. It turned out that in the middle of the main courtyard, there was a brick platform on which sat a large jar of homemade soy sauce. Removing the jar and demolishing the platform revealed a hoard of silver. The bandits filled burlap sacks, hoisted them onto poles, and made off with their loot. Afterwards, the old man told others that they had lost over ten thousand dollars.

In Shanxi, the practice of hiding silver was even more prevalent. One family built a secret cellar in their home, where they melted all their silver dollars into liquid silver and poured it in. Once solidified, it formed a huge silver ingot, easier to preserve and less likely to be stolen. One year, unfortunately, news of this secret reached some mutinous soldiers, who swarmed to the house and broke open the cellar. However, faced with the solid silver, they could find no way to take it. After some futile hammering, they left empty-handed.

Someone Jumps into the Water

— Shui Rong

The person has been rescued and is now vomiting on a chair. We don't know what else he threw up besides water. How dark it is here! There's no moon tonight. The light from the white lamp is blocked by the onlookers. A police officer waves his hand, shouting, "Move back, move back!" But no one listens. Those in the back are desperately trying to push forward.

Someone is striking a match. Everyone cranes their necks to see what kind of person this suicidal individual is. In the brief flame, I only catch a glimpse: black cloth jacket, black socks, old black sneakers. His physique and attire make me believe he is around twenty years old. "So young!" I couldn't help but exclaim.

Several Americans are leaning against the railing, discussing how the life preservers are positioned too far away. One asks me, "Does he have any friends here?" I reply, "No."

A terrifying silence reigns over the space. The world-weary person is no longer making a sound. I fear something bad is about to happen. The autumn wind is sobbing through the plane trees.

Finally, the rescue team arrives, causing a stir. Watching them place the dying man on a stretcher and carry him out of the park, the onlookers disperse, talking and laughing.

Alone in this place, I gaze at the pile of discarded belongings on the ground, then at the vast, dark, oily Huangpu River, feeling an inexplicable sorrow. Why would someone try to end their own life? Doesn't everyone have a desire to live? And he is so young. He doesn't seem to have been driven to it by love, so the most likely reason must be economic pressure. If that's the case, aren't we—aren't we all partly responsible? Human progress means the improvement of everyone's life. Isn't suicide a disgrace to humanity? And what am I to make of the onlookers' laughter and chatter?

Let me pray for that unfortunate person!

Literary News: In recent years, the public has become increasingly interested in modern songs, and the sales of songbooks have increased daily. The "Collection of Songs of Autumn Memories," recently published by the Fine Arts Bookstore, is the new work of Mr. Yin Yiqiu, a former professor at the China Conservatory of Music. It contains over twenty new songs, such as "Waves," "New Little Shepherd Boy," and "Labor is Sacred," as well as thirty-four older works such as "National Flower," "What is Love," and "I Cannot Forget You," all proofread by Mr. Yin himself more than three times to ensure accuracy. It is now available from the Zhongqingji Bookstore on Four Horses Road, and all bookstores in this city and other locales have it for sale.

Romance of the Three Kingdoms

— Yang Yusheng

Random Notes on Storytelling

The novel *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* can truly be considered a household name in China. If one says that men who have read *Dream of the Red Chamber* want to emulate Jia Baoyu, and women want to emulate Lin Daiyu, then I dare to assert that those who have read *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* all want to emulate Zhuge Kongming!

Because readers of *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* all sympathize with the Shu Han, hoping that Liu Xuande can "rebuild the mountains and rivers"! And Kongming is the pillar of Shu Han, so their attention naturally focuses on him. Therefore, some say that after reading the part in *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* where Kongming dies at Wuzhang Plains, they can't bear to read any further! Even reading on will only deepen their lament! The direction of people's hearts is truly profound!

In fact, those who stop reading after Kongming's death at Wuzhang Plains are still quite patient! If it were me, after Lü Ziming crossed the river in disguise, the rest of *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* wouldn't need to be read! Because after the loss of Jingzhou, the Shu Han's foothold was gone. Even with Kongming's talent, he could only maneuver around Qishan, ultimately leading to a partial peace and inevitable downfall! This is the factual proof that "Han and traitors cannot coexist."

Kongming foresaw all of this long ago! In his Longzhong Plan, he clearly determined that the world would be divided into three parts, but he still followed Liu Xuande desperately to fight the rebels! To restore the Han Dynasty! Giving his all! Until his death! Kongming's ability to leave a lasting name is not due to his accomplishments or his talent, but to his extremely devoted and loyal heart. This is what many of our unmotivated descendants should deeply encourage themselves to emulate!

Let me repeat a few of Kongming's famous words to you all! During the Longzhong Plan, he said to Liu Xuande, "The north allows Cao Cao to gain the opportune time, the east allows Sun Quan to gain the geographical advantage, and the general can take Xichuan and occupy the people's harmony." It can be seen that Liu Adou was able to be a muddle-headed emperor in Sichuan for more than forty years entirely relying on the power of "people's harmony"! If a country loses both the opportune time and the geographical advantage, and also loses the people's harmony, I want to ask you all, what power does it rely on to survive in this dog-eat-dog world!

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-One: Gently Relying on Others, Passing the Courtyard to Admire the Moon's Beauty; Ardent Teaching of the Son-in-Law, Listening to the Lion's Roar from the Next Room

The woman yields the path: I insist on interfering, if the one with the surname Jia is mistreating him, I, Jin Rongxue, will file a lawsuit against him. Fortunately, there is a specialist stationed here in Little Western Paradise to investigate human morality. If one wants to file a complaint, one can do so here at the hotel. The bureau chief says: Hey, sister-in-law, you don't need to interfere here, you should leave. Following these words, the Hu sister-in-law grabbed the wall, passing the window, slowly walking away, head bowed. However, the woman in the western suit immediately ran with the sound of her high heel shoes, grabbing the Hu sister-in-law’s hands. One can see her face clearly now, covered in a thick layer of powder like lime. However, amidst the thick powder, uneven purple bumps are scattered all over. Both eyebrows are cleanly plucked, but two thick scars of skin remain, and she painted ink lines on top of the scars. Her eyes are as big as walnuts, with a radish flower on her right eyelid. Her nose is quite high, but below her nose, her two thick lips are flipped inside out, revealing two rows of messy teeth. She says: What are you afraid of? If I don't let you leave, no one would dare to make you leave. Do you think he is a boss? That is nothing. Without me, he could not be a boss. Just come in with me to talk. The Hu sister-in-law had famously small feet. How could she endure such a powerful tug? In an unbalanced position, she was tugged into the house. When Bei Hai heard the wife asking the Hu sister-in-law, his bottom, was tense and tight. As the Hu sister-in-law ran out, he exhaled a breath of air. His bottom revealed a hint of disappointment. As the Hu sister-in-law re-entered, he lifted his dejected face again, and smiled to Zhi Qian: At least like this, he can come up with some way. (370)

Miscellaneous Remarks

Sitting in the Empty Courtyard in the Rain

— Luo Dian

My mood is like a gloomy rainy day. Even if there is a sliver of blue sky, it is soon blown away by the wind, turning into a vast, pale haze. My whole body is enveloped in layers of pale mist. I cannot see the sun's smile, nor can I hear the breath of the human world. Because in the vast empty courtyard, only I remain. If the thrush under the reed curtain occasionally sings a charming new song, this almost mocking sound only further emphasizes the stillness of midday. I am somewhat afraid to hear it. Truly, there is nothing more lonely than the faint sighs of the reeds occasionally rustling on the shore. I understand this environment. It is best to sit near the window, pour a cup of bitter tea, and watch the steam rise from the tea leaves and slowly dissipate. There is no need to study the physics of pressure, nor to seek elegant verses, much less to reminisce about the past or predict the future. Perhaps I can temporarily forget myself and seep into a more magical, more profound dream, thus finding happiness. However, though I am lonely, I am also alone. I feel the chill. How can I know that someone is rushing to a school far away in western Shanghai during this public holiday because of my powerlessness! Is it right to call him away from home, away from me, in the gloomy early winter, when the wind has grown sharp and the rain is falling madly? And does he have the heart to leave home and me? Let me think leisurely: the person running on the rainy street does not hate the excessive amount of work he is carrying. And I, sitting at home doing nothing, dare to complain of loneliness? Isolation? Even if I am truly bored, I deserve to suffer! Can I chew half a word? I must awaken my conscience. A young child is searching for food for me at this moment! Does he not understand the "sadness of shadows"? And he doesn't even speak Guangzhou dialect!

So I smile. Happy raindrops shower my forehead. Carrying a spirit that is lighter than benzoin, I gradually stroll into the courtyard. On the white stones of the courtyard, pearls of light dance, and I breathe in a refreshing, sweet breeze. My limbs and eyes feel comfortable and clear. A refreshing cold air, along with two droplets, strikes my hair, flies into my skin, and penetrates deep into my heart. I feel especially energetic and excited, as if my eyes, having just escaped from a bitter prison, have been struck by a golden arrow of sunlight.

All hatred of oneself or others is caused by unwillingness to forgive. There is nothing that cannot be resolved if you can take a step back. Even the world could be without war. But regardless of so-called sages or rogues, few have any interest in considering "forgiveness," so the blood of struggle forever satirizes the armor of civilization. "True love" is nowhere to be seen between people!

Thank you for this refreshing winter rain, which has enlightened me with extraordinary wisdom. I pull up a rattan chair and sit by the lotus flower pot, letting the spiritual rain of the day irrigate the brains of ignorant people.

Everyone who hears of lotus flowers will think of the fragrant breeze of June. In this season of scattered leaves, it seems unnecessary to mention them. But precisely for this reason, I am even more willing to pay attention to them. I still remember when I first moved here, this courtyard was full of lotus flowers. In the muddy water of each flower pot, small goldfish swam back and forth, shimmering among the green stems and red flowers, very beautiful. Whenever it rained, raindrops poured from the lotus leaves, dripping into the pot, and the small goldfish would open their mouths, instinctively swallowing, then flick their tails and swim away gracefully. This beautiful impression is truly difficult for me to forget. But now, the lotus roots have long been ground into powder and used as food; the lotus stems have been broken and sent to pharmacies. Where are the flowers now? Even those exquisite goldfish have gradually died, leaving very few. And the few that remain have been moved into the white porcelain bowls in the study, as ornaments for the windows, because they cannot bear the cold. Of course, they cannot absorb natural spring dew and seem to show signs of decline. It is hard to say if their fate will allow them to survive until the New Year. Flowers and fish, on this rainy day, cannot help but make me feel sad for myself! Moreover, the dried-up lotus pot is gradually filled with clear water, reflecting a thin face?

Commercial News

Money Market: Eager Buyers Cause Premium to Rise Another Five Yuan Three, Repeatedly Breaking Through the Fifty Yuan Mark, Rumors of Benefits Lead to Increasing Market Activity

Yesterday, the gold market saw active trading, with the Mobil Oil Company settling US dollars, the previous market stabilizing after a flat start, eager buyers in the market, firm and bullish sentiment, and further gains driven by rumors of cash exports, pushing the price above fifty yuan. The trend was quite active. Early in the morning, the overseas silver market saw no change in both the UK and the US. The forward silver price at Montreaux was unchanged, up one cent and down two cents respectively. Exchange rates fluctuated, and the London spot gold was unchanged. The London large foot gold also remained very stable, so the market sentiment was neutral. In addition, the Central Bank's announced rates were unchanged for both the UK and the US, the customs gold unit was unchanged, and the standard premium was listed at 1146.9 yuan. The preliminary trading outside the market opened at around 44 yuan, showing a peaceful state. Although it slightly fell after opening, buying activity picked up due to Mobil Oil Company settling spot US dollars, and the price was quickly pulled up. The HSBC's rates remained flat for both the UK and the US. There were many transactions mid-session, then the market tightened as the Bank of Japan and HSBC and others scrambled for spot pounds, and the buying momentum surged, gradually rising. The price once approached the 50 yuan mark, but large players took profits at the high and banks filled orders at the high price, hindering the upward momentum. The announced silver balancing tax was unchanged, and the general trend flattened. Later, the market slightly dipped as buyers took profits, but the prediction on the silver import tax was unchanged and had little impact. Buying momentum remained, and the price was easily pulled up after the dip. The afternoon trend was stable. The market was further strengthened in the later session by the increasing rumors of cash exports, and the price broke out above 50 yuan. Chinese merchants and merchants from the mainland scrambled to buy, and the market sentiment was positive and bullish, so the price rose step by step. Banks took advantage of the high prices to fill orders, and the exchange rate was strong and then flat, gradually falling back. However, there was a great deal of struggle in the middle of the session. The price then retreated below 50 yuan due to the constant profit-taking by large players. The initial report of the silver import tax was unchanged, and then up one anna, but because there were still many buyers chasing the price after the dip, the price was easily pulled up again. The second report of the silver import tax was a decrease of three annas, and the market fluctuated. Ultimately, the market closed below 50 yuan due to excessive profit-taking. The forward premium was about 8 yuan yesterday.

The market opened in the morning at 1144.2 yuan, down one cent from the previous Saturday. Although Huixiang Heng and Yu Qianchang Xiang advanced to 4.8 yuan, Dadecheng, Chunyuan Yong, Richang Wanfeng still sold at 3.2 yuan. Mobil settled spot US dollars at 8125, and Shunmao, Yifeng, Yongfuxing, Yongheng, Yu Dadecheng, Dafa Yong and others came to buy. Although HSBC's rates were flat, they still rose to 6.4 yuan. Huixiang and Dadecheng took advantage of the high prices to sell, bringing the price down to 5.3 yuan. HSBC bought spot pounds at half a penny. Fuxing Yong, Dadecheng, Chunyuan Yongfu, Yu Huixiang, Heng Yu, Lichang Richang, Qingfa, Yong Yi Feng, Yong all rushed to buy contracts, gradually rising to 8.7 yuan. Dadecheng and Wanfeng sold contracts, retreating to 7.8 yuan. Hengyu, Chunyuan Yong, Dadecheng, Yuansheng Yong, Tongfu still advanced and rose to 9.8 yuan. Fuxing Yong forcefully sold at the high price, and Dingkang and Dadecheng also sold. Citibank and Maccary filled January US dollar contracts at 4375. Richang advanced and resold, bringing the price down to 7.6 yuan. The silver balancing tax was unchanged. The market sentiment was then peaceful and there were many transactions. Although Deli, Lichang, and Huixiang advanced to 8.7 yuan, Fuxing Yong, Dadecheng, and retail investors sold again at 6.9 yuan. Hengyu, Demao, Yong Dadecheng bought contracts at the low price. Banks still bought January US dollars at half a yuan, rising to 8.3 yuan. Richang supplied contracts, bringing the price down to 7.2 yuan. Hengyu and Shenfeng still advanced to 8.3 yuan. Richang and Wanfeng sold and traded a lot. Qingfa Yong, Shenkang, Chunyuan Yong Dadecheng came to sell, retreating to 6.4 yuan. The silver import tax prediction was unchanged and had no impact. Tongtaichang, Hengyu, Richang, Dadecheng, and Shenfeng came to buy, gradually pulling the price up. The market closed at noon at 1147.9 yuan, and was more stable after the market close.

The market opened in the later session at 1149.8 yuan. Richang, Shenfeng, Chunyuan Yong Shenkang came to buy from 9.6 yuan, rising to 50.8 yuan. Fuxing Yong sold, bringing the price down to 02 cents. Fuyu, Yuansheng Yong, Chunyuan Yong Hengyu, Fuxing Yong still advanced, and Tianchengxiang also paid, rising 1.8 yuan. Hengyu Yifeng Yong sold, bringing the price down to 07 cents. Fuxing Yong Chunyuan Yong advanced again to 1.5 yuan. Yifeng Yong, Richang Huixiang, Dadecheng Yuanchang Yong Hengchang Yong sold a lot, retreating to 49.5 yuan. Chunyuan Yong came to buy, rising to 50.7 yuan. Hengyu Fuxing Yong sold contracts, falling to 49.2 yuan. The initial report of the silver import tax was unchanged, up one anna, and the situation lingered. Dadecheng, Tongfu Chunyuan, Yong Yongfeng, Yuansheng Yong Lichang, Fuxing Yong Fuyu bought contracts one after another, gradually rising back to 51.2 yuan. Hengchang Yong Dadecheng sold contracts at the high price, bringing the price down to 50 yuan. The second report of the silver import tax was a decrease of three annas, and the situation remained stable. Later, Qingfa Yong Huixiang sold, retreating to 49.2 yuan. Tongtaichang Hengyu Qianyuan Yong bought contracts, rising to 50.7 yuan. Richang and others still sold at the high price, bringing the price down to 49.6 yuan. The market closed at 1149.7 yuan.

The settlement price was the Central Bank's standard premium, which was listed at 1146.9 yuan. The closing price was about three yuan higher, and more than five yuan higher than the previous Saturday. The account price for this month was 1139 yuan, and for January it was 1148 yuan. The water replenishment for the morning was 1139 yuan, and for the afternoon it was 141 yuan. The price of pure gold was reduced by one yuan, to 1143.2 yuan. The spot market remained stable. Tianjin goods and boiled red goods added four yuan each, but there were still few transactions because the forward premium was not large. Customers were happy to point them out. Yesterday, Yuanmaoyong posted forward premiums to Dafeng Heng of 35 contracts at 8.7 yuan, Yingfeng Heng posted forward premiums to Chunyuan Yong of 42 contracts, Dingtai 7 contracts at 8.5 yuan, Chunyuan Yong posted forward premiums to Yicheng 42 contracts at 8 yuan, and Dingtai posted forward premiums to Lifeng 7 contracts at 8.3 yuan.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking

Uniform Hotel Room Rates Established by Hotel Association

— Zi Nan

Having been in Shanghai for over five years, I believe I have some knowledge of the rise of Shanghai's hotel industry. If we take a stroll down Tibet Road, we'll see that it's almost entirely lined with hotels. Five years ago, there weren't nearly as many, and certainly none as grand and luxurious as they are now.

Four or five years ago, passing through Tibet Road late at night, what impression would we get? Broadly speaking, it was a city that never slept. Even at two or three in the morning, the sounds of dice games, dominoes, and women's songs mixed with stringed instruments filled the streets, with bright lights shining from every window.

(Shanghai's hotels don't cater to "travelers." Hotels are merely havens for Shanghai residents to indulge in entertainment and leisure, which invariably involves drinking, prostitution, and gambling.)

Now, if you pass through there at midnight, you'll notice that the bright lights in every window that were common four or five years ago are now rarely seen. Although the lights at the entrances remain, even brighter than before, they are hardly a sign of luxury. Instead, they probably signify "pay by the day" or a discount rate.

After the economic downturn hit, the countryside was the first to suffer. Shanghai, being a so-called economic, commercial, and cultural-political center, initially showed signs of hyperemia when the downturn first arrived. This hyperemia, however, soon turned into edema as anemia in other sectors deepened. While things might appear the same on the surface, the situation is actually no better than in the countryside.

Recently, these symptoms have become impossible to conceal and have gradually spread from other businesses to the hotel industry.

In the closing years of the century, the extravagance of the petty bourgeoisie and the wealthy was a defining characteristic. Seeing the decline of their class and unable to resist, they embraced hedonism, desperately seeking material and spiritual enjoyment and stimulation. Hotels, as havens for drinking, prostitution, and gambling, became the best places to go.

However, in recent years, with the increasing economic panic, the petty bourgeoisie has found it increasingly difficult to sustain their lifestyle. Consequently, large hotels have had to resort to offers like "buy one night, get one free" and "discounts" to attract customers.

These "buy one, get one free" or "buy one, get two free" and "discount" schemes have disrupted room rates within the industry. As a result, the Hotel Association has established six measures to "uniform hotel room rates" and "implement discounts."

However, whether the standardization of room rates can be achieved through the Hotel Association's resolutions remains to be seen. While the resolution to "prevent disguised standard discount violations, such as gifts, after implementing an 80% discount rate" can be enforced by the Hotel Association, how can we guarantee that individual hotels won't lower their original prices? Furthermore, even if room rates are set by the Hotel Association "based on cost considerations to determine a balanced price," can this guarantee improvement in business?

If the fundamental problems remain unresolved, what is the use of merely achieving "uniform room rates"?

And these so-called fundamental problems arise from the social structure.

Winter Scene

— Bei Hua

The night is so long...

The river surface is silent. The water reflects a silvery-gray light, rippling and making faint sounds. Ships are anchored in the middle of the river like monsters, their black smokestacks obscuring half the moon, casting large shadows. The road in front of the Jianghai Customs House, except for the occasional passing car or two, shows little sign of life. Facing the Great Clock Tower, the patrolling police officer sighs.

In the misty air, his drowsy eyes seem to see something—yes, he sees his wife at home, her affectionate, almond-shaped eyes wide open, lying in bed waiting for his return. And his son's little face, so sweetly dreaming. He has a warm home, yet he stands here, facing the biting river wind.

The wind, carrying whispers from the fields of Pudong, blows past the shoulders of the God of Peace. In the wind's whistling, he finally wakes up. He looks up at the time: the Great Clock Tower is striking half past three.

The chime awakens a homeless child who has been dozing off in a corner of the warehouse. Rubbing his eyes, he feels cold and finds it impossible to fall back asleep. He nudges Xiao Liu Zi next to him, but the boy remains half-dead, unresponsive. Just then, his keen senses tell him that someone is approaching—the footsteps are getting closer and clearer. So he slaps Xiao Liu Zi hard! "The police are coming!" he shouts, grabbing Xiao Liu Zi and running away.

The world is vast, yet they have nowhere to rest. Under the pale lights outside the park, these two small souls have dark, gaunt faces. Hunger and cold make them shiver. How can their tattered and thin clothes withstand the cold of this late November night?

This is the time when people who enjoy pleasure and those who are used for pleasure are riding home in cars to rest. "Let's go to the bridge over there and make a few cents to buy flatbread tomorrow!" Xiao Liu Zi says. It took a lot of hard work for them to get the chance to pull rickshaws at the bridge; now, it has become their only means of survival. As they walk, they stare at the black water of the Suzhou Creek, their small hearts frozen cold.

On this side of the bridge, they wait for customers to take them to the other side, earning one or two copper coins from the late-night travelers, which they pocket in their half-torn clothes. No one shows them any sympathy, in this world where everyone lacks a sympathetic heart. A young dancer, emerging from a nightclub into the cold night, sits in a rickshaw and relaxes her body, sore from being embraced. She has no time to spare for Xiao Liu Zi. A drunken sailor, with his hat askew, covering one eye, laughs inexplicably. Xiao Liu Zi has no choice but to hide to the side, feeling sorry for the rickshaw puller struggling under the sailor's boots. A prostitute with an unusually ugly face, unable to find any customers, stands blankly on the bridge, looking at the sky and then at the river, as if unable to find a place to go, whether it be heaven or hell...

The night is so long; it seems like dawn will never come, and the cold intensifies.

The frost on the roofs will not melt until the sun rises tomorrow. The power lines and streetlights accompany the loneliness of the city. In the distance, around the corner, it seems someone is walking by, the sound of footsteps breaking the silence of the street. The sleeping city, wake up!

The Shoe-Shining Boy

— Lin Na

(A Manila Story)

It was a clear morning. Heavy trucks had already begun to rumble down the dusty, coal-reeking asphalt road. Xi Luo, a homeless child, was just waking up from a slumber on a cement bench in the First Municipal Park. He gently opened his dry, weary eyes, the soft sunlight piercing them, causing him to blink constantly. He thought: It's late! Damn it..., and then he hurriedly got off the cement bench, using his dirty sleeve to wipe the sleep from his eyes and the dew from his face. Suddenly, he felt a strange noise in his stomach and realized he was hungry.

Just then, the monotonous cough of the park keeper, old Ling Luo, echoed dully from under a row of plane trees. Feeling uneasy and frightened, he quickly grabbed his small wooden stool and wooden box, hidden under the cement bench, stood up, and tried to run along the path leading to the street. But before he could take a step, he heard the park keeper, old Ling Luo, shout his familiar, fierce, and slightly hoarse command:

"Stop right there, you little brat!"

As soon as he turned his head, the park keeper's rough wooden stick flashed in the soft sunlight. Trembling slightly, he forgot his usual habit of making faces or sticking out his tongue at the park keeper, and instead took off running towards the exit.

The streets were crowded with office workers and factory workers with worried faces. Shiny cars honked loudly in the middle of the street and sped away, while horses pulling broken carriages snorted and whinnied, raised their tails, and kicked their hind legs, but when the angry drivers whipped them hard on their backs, they stood still and silent.

Xi Luo was now lost in the crowd. He felt terribly tired and depressed, and almost stumbled on the sidewalk several times, but thanks to God's grace, he was pushed along by the hurrying pedestrians. His head was heavy and muddled, and he couldn't help but think of things from a few years ago.

It was an unsettling June day. Manila was rife with cholera. His father, a coachman, came home early one day, complaining of a headache, and died three days later. His mother also caught the infection and died the day after his father. Thus, twelve-year-old Xi Luo became an orphan. The fifty-two-year-old Mrs. Moro, who lived next door, said she was doing it for God's sake, and limped around, begging his close and distant neighbors, saying:

"For the sake of the merciful God, save this homeless orphan..."

The elderly coachman, Fu Xi, generously took out money from his shriveled pouch and donated it. Then everyone else donated too. So Mrs. Moro prepared a small wooden stool and a black wooden box (which contained brushes, shoe polish, and rags) for him and told him to go out into the streets to shine shoes for people and make a living.

And now? His home, Mrs. Moro, in the name of God, had moved into, with her eight-year-old child. He was now forced to retreat to the First Municipal Park to spend the night…

He slowly walked along Rosario Avenue, then turned into Brooke Square. However, not a single customer called out to him, "Xi Luo, come here!" Then an American gentleman in a suit gestured for him to come over. He hurriedly agreed and ran across.

Now, the American gentleman sat on his little wooden stool, his legs stretched straight out on his black wooden box, smoking a cigar contentedly. And Xi Luo knelt in front of him, carefully applying shoe polish, brushing, and shining his shoes. Gradually, the dirty shoes became shiny and gleaming. The American gentleman, satisfied, took the cigar butt from his mouth and threw it on the ground, where another person immediately picked it up and put it in his mouth. Xi Luo knelt in front of him, looking up and wiping the sweat from his face with his dirty sleeve. He was very happy, because he would soon have a full breakfast.

A tram rumbled loudly from afar and stopped at the station. The American gentleman proudly stepped onto the tram, but forgot to pay Xi Luo for shining his shoes. Xi Luo was shocked.

"Sir, you forgot, the money for shining the shoes!"

But before he could react, he was kicked hard in his skinny butt by the shiny shoe tip. He stumbled backward, still wanting to chase after him, but the tram had already rumbled away, leaving behind a contemptuous burst of laughter in the coal-reeking air. One of his compatriots even stuck a slick, oily head out of the window and cursed him harshly.

"You little wretch, serves you right!"

"Serves me right? I earned it with my own strength!" Xi Luo thought, and sadly took his little wooden stool and black wooden box to a quiet place, where he cried secretly.

— Jiang Mi

The two fighting dogs, Zhuanxu and Gonggong, were fighting to become the leader, to be revered in the south, and they argued there, one saying: I am a man ordained by heaven, God specially ordered me to unify the world! One said: I don't know what to boast about heaven and earth, I just want to be the emperor following my heart. These two fighting dogs, both holding the determination that there can be only one sun in the sky and only one emperor among the people, the result of the roar is, of course, to use force to compete in length. "Wild Geese Descending on the Sandy Banks" can be described as an unparalleled tragedy. When Chang Ma and Xu Weibang's "Pear Blossoms in a Rainstorm" was premiered, many praised its refined and unconventional style. Seeing "Wild Geese Descending on the Sandy Banks" today, it is even more filled with poetic and artistic flair, and its poignant and sorrowful aspects are even more pronounced than the previous film.

Yang Xiaozhong's new script, "Wildcat," has been completed.

To act in a way that one naturally sheds tears during a sad scene is inherently difficult. Among Chinese actors, only a few can achieve this. Wang Hanlun, who had been away from the silver screen for a long time, recently filmed a tragic scene for "Tears on the Faded Red." Ms. Hanlun actually burst into tears, crying so sorrowfully that it truly moved people's hearts.

Han Langan has taken a ten-day leave of absence to return home. As a result, "Three Modern Men" only has two modern men working on the set.

Fei Mu's work, "Fragrant Snow Sea," is being dubbed and prepared for release in France due to demand from French theaters. All musical arrangements and necessary textual preparations have been completed and will be sent abroad within days. The music for the film is entirely Eastern in style.

"Clouds Over Abyssinia" Premieres

—Abyssinia's Strange Customs and Exotic Scenes All Captured on Film—

The long-awaited topical and realistic epic "Wings Over Ethiopia" has been scheduled to premiere at the Grand Theater today. The film's content, concerning Abyssinia, can be said to depict everything from modern to ancient warfare, from civilized to savage regions. All the strange customs and exotic scenes of Abyssinia are captured in the film. The most peculiar and interesting is a special custom of the natives in southern Abyssinia: a woman can have one husband and five lovers. On the fifth day after the wedding, the groom must leave his room, allowing the bride's first lover to enter. When the husband sleeps at home, he must place his long spear in front of the door to indicate that someone is inside, preventing others from intruding. In short, those who care about world affairs should appreciate this work.

Shen Bao Architectural Weekly

An Exploration of Ancient Bath Garden Architecture (Part 1)

—Sun Zongwen

—One of the Crystallizations of Roman National Architectural Art—

"Bath Garden Architecture" (Thermae Architecture) is a seemingly unfamiliar term; although it is also an artwork among the world's buildings. The reason why it is not generally noticed by people is due to two factors: First, in terms of history: Because architecture is a "historical record"; so the appearance of a certain type of building is sufficient to represent the prosperity of this country and the characteristics of its people; so it can be said that it is a crystallization of the times, environment, and national character. Throughout history, both in China and abroad, the thing that mankind is most affected by is religion? Therefore, the most magnificent and splendid buildings, and the ones that people most like to build, are also "religious buildings." Let's look! From the beginning of the world until today, which period of time has the general public not devoted themselves to religious buildings? Since the pyramids, which have existed for thousands of years, there have been the mysterious temples of ancient Egypt, the magnificent temples of Greece, the solemn temples of Rome, and the great and quiet Christian churches of modern times; countless religious buildings have appeared in the world! And what is even stranger is that our architectural art seems to be a substitute for religious art, because every part of it symbolizes religious spiritual meaning. The reason is that in the past history, the greatest force influencing design was religion. We have proven that architecture is a "historical record," so the center of a world architectural history is based on religious architecture; and the "bath garden architecture" that we are talking about now has nothing to do with religion, so it is no wonder that it is ignored by the general public. Second, in terms of art; the world's architecture is centered on religion, so artistic skills are particularly focused on religious buildings. "Bath gardens" are a niche thing, and few great and impressive masterpieces have appeared since ancient times, so they contribute little to art itself; as a result, those who study architectural art in the world have reduced their interest in it; the result is that it has become a not very important material, left in our architectural history.

Since bath gardens are not important buildings, then why should we study them? That's right, modern bath gardens are not worth exploring; but ancient bath gardens are really worth studying. In ancient times, there were bath gardens that were as magnificent as palaces, as mysterious as temples, and as splendid as shrines, and perhaps even more precious, more beautiful, and more delicate works than religious buildings! Where are these crystallizations of art hidden? Then we can say without thinking: "Beautiful Rome." Okay, let's take the bath garden architectural art of Rome as the focus of our exploration!

Roman culture, although inherited from Greek culture, also has different aspects; because Romans are a practical nation. Their imagination is far less abundant than that of the Greeks, but their calm, composed, and common-sense minds are one of the characteristics of their national character; and Romans are rich in public nature, so public buildings are particularly developed. Public hygiene was also advanced at that time; therefore, bath garden architecture appeared in various places one after another. The Roman era can be said to be the golden age of "bath garden architecture"; its exquisite techniques and beautiful art are no less than the "temples" of Greece; moreover, it is one of the crystallizations of Roman national architectural art!

Romans especially value obedience, so they are particularly obedient to their emperors; they believe that the emperor's power is greater than everything, therefore, the palace buildings in various places are particularly grand and magnificent. As bath gardens are subsidiary buildings of palaces, the construction of bath gardens also flourished accordingly; this is one of the reasons why bath gardens developed. The beginning of bath gardens can be traced back to Egypt; however, the scale was rudimentary. By the time the Greek city government opened, people's living standards improved, and society paid attention to hygiene, bath gardens were strongly promoted; when Rome rose, bath gardens can be regarded as the true construction period, because many great masterpieces appeared one after another at that time, especially during the reign of Emperor Nero (Nero), the grand scale of its bath gardens, the materials collected from all countries, and the craftsmanship exhausted by all craftsmen, were sufficient to represent the honor of the Roman Empire. I remember there was a movie called "Romance in the Palace"; several interior scenes were bath gardens of the imperial palace. The splendor of the set and the exquisiteness of the carvings were truly breathtaking. From the screen, we can also imagine a glimpse of the architectural art of bath gardens at that time. Although Europeans and Americans today pay attention to skills, when they see the port gardens of Rome, they will probably be amazed!

How to Utilize a House

—Written by Qian Zhenjie, Translated by Zhang Guangzheng

A house is a container for life. However, the family life within this container is constantly changing. For example, as time progresses, the head of the household changes. If the family's income increases, it will lead to an increase in interests and hobbies. Regarding the house, there will often be requests for the establishment or separation of children's rooms and the father's study.

Therefore, even if the house was built under extremely thorough planning, after a period of time, it will naturally feel insufficient to use. Moreover, most of the salary earners nowadays live in rented houses. The inconvenience they feel in their daily lives can be imagined.

However, once a house is built, it becomes real estate. The only procedures required after that are maintenance. However, when tenants move out, most landlords are afraid of the trouble of compensating for these maintenance and repair costs, so they are unwilling to allow tenants to modify the house at will, and often impose restrictions on this point. Due to these reasons, even if one wants to modify the unsatisfactory parts to adapt to one's life and achieve a more comfortable degree, it is impossible.

In this way, within the scope where remodeling or major repairs are impossible, is there no more clever way to live? The following are simple methods of living in a house comfortably and well without spending a lot of money, relying only on good arrangement.

(1) The Locking Style of the Doorway

In order to prevent accidents, it is best to install a Western-style door. Open a small hole in a part of the door panel or wall, install glass to act as a peephole, and it is best to cover it with a thin and beautiful silk cloth on the inside. After seeing who the visitor is through this look, one can open the door and welcome them in with peace of mind.

Next, regarding locks. If the door style is single-leaf, there is a type called a "positive lock." Fasten the center of the handle to the side, lower the key from the inside, and it will be difficult to open from the outside. The handling method is also extremely convenient, as long as one takes it along when entering or exiting, the outside will not be pushed open.

There is also a type called a safety lock, which has the advantage that it is not easy to open from the outside. And the opening of the door has a certain width. The lock is made of gold. Many households in New York use it.

(2) Install Screens

In new construction areas, mosquitoes fly in swarms every summer night, which is extremely annoying. If fine wire mesh is installed on the window, it can be prevented. If so, one can both enjoy the cool breeze of summer nights and defend against mosquito attacks. And the installation cost is not high, and the benefits are very considerable. Made into a screen frame, it is easy to remove when not in use.

Also, if the house has shutters and glass windows, replacing the glass windows with screens can also achieve the above purpose.

(3) Improving Kitchen Efficiency

In the kitchen, cover the gas appliances and stove equipment used for cooking with a lead-skin cover, lead it to the chimney, and install a ventilation fan at the end to remove odors outdoors. If a small electric fan is installed, the ventilation effect can be good.

Fish bones, meat bones, vegetable scraps, and other waste are very troublesome to handle, finely broken, and very easy to contaminate the kitchen. Use a lead pipe inclined from the inside of the kitchen, through the wall, to the outside. First, prepare a large bucket to collect waste, and pour it from the pipe from time to time. This is also a better way.

(4) Washroom, Bathroom, and Toilet

Houses with specially built washrooms are mostly quite complete. As for general small residences, most people use the kitchen for washing their faces every morning. However, it is unclean and inconvenient to use the place where tableware and food are handled. Therefore, it is best to set up washing utensils in a corner of the bathroom. If the bathroom is not equipped or is small, it is best to set up washing utensils next to the water pipe at one end of the outer corridor. It is very simple and not unsightly. Especially for developing children's habit of washing hands before meals, it is more suitable.

Hang a cloth bag of the same color as the wall on the bathroom wall, which can be used to place toothbrushes, toothpaste, soap, etc., which is also very suitable.

If the toilet is three to five square feet wide, a shelf that can hold flower pots, bouquets, and incense burners can be placed in one corner. In this way, the unclean place will be changed into a better and more pleasant place. The fragrance is hated by flies, so it can also drive away a lot of flies.

(5) Study and Children's Room

To effectively use a small study, it is not wrong to put more bookshelves. Just make sure that the books can be arranged in an orderly manner without hindering the opening and closing of the door and access.

As for children's rooms, the furnishings are best simple and constantly changing. At the entrance, set up a larger wall mirror and washing utensils to cultivate children's cleanliness habits. Indeed, children's moving sand and carrying stones, dragging mud and water, often make the interior of the house unclean. But this is the nature of children's activity, and it is not a matter of being too forced.

(6) Utilization Under the Eaves

The southeast-facing window is the best way for sunlight to enter the house in one day, so try to make it as spacious as possible. And most new-style houses have windows open in this direction. In summer, it can introduce cool breezes, and in winter, it can avoid direct cold winds and maintain an appropriate temperature. On the contrary, the best thing under the eaves facing northwest is to plant some flowers and trees, which can make the environment more beautiful.

Factory Building Design (Part 2)

—Bo Ping

(1) Speaking of single-story buildings, they occupy the largest area. If it were in Shanghai, where land prices are extremely high, it would be immediately uneconomical. However, because their structures are interconnected, once one part is completed, it can be sent to the second part. In this way, manufacturing is very procedural, easy to manage, and the light is always relatively sufficient, and the air is also very fresh.

(2) Multi-story! Because land prices are too expensive, our factory buildings have several or even dozens of floors. In this way, there are more workplaces, but boilers, engines, etc., must be placed on the first floor to avoid danger. The upper floors are only suitable for light work.

(3) Large-span type! This type of building is most suitable for factories with many workers, such as ironworking, etc.

(4) Separate type - It is best to separate the buildings of dangerous factories part by part, because if one room has a danger, it will avoid affecting other parts, such as gunpowder factories and match factories, etc.

(3) Choice of Materials

In modern factory construction, safety is the main design consideration. Therefore, countries have certain regulations on the materials for factory construction. The commonly used ones include wood, stone, iron, and reinforced concrete:

(1) Wood - Not very strong, but the price is extremely cheap, construction is rapid, easy to repair, and many factories that are short-term and have no dangers are happy to use it.

(2) Stone - Does not catch fire, has extremely strong resistance, but transportation is not easy, depending on the distance of local stone production.

(3) Iron - Iron-style buildings are rare in China. It is certainly not easy to catch fire, but it is very easy to conduct heat. Its advantage is that construction is rapid and repairs are few.

(4) Reinforced concrete is the latest type of building material. In addition to being solid, it is not easy to catch fire and does not require repairs, but the price is a bit too expensive.

(4) Light Design

The design of light is also very important. It is best to use natural sunlight. Therefore, the design of the roof and skylights should be carefully considered. The design of the roof is for this purpose. The common one used is the sawtooth roof. When it comes to the design of windows, it is necessary to ensure (1) sufficient light that is spread throughout the room, (2) avoid direct sunlight, so that there is reflected light.

(5) Safety Equipment Design

(1) Emergency exit - Each building should have three to five emergency exits according to building regulations. The door can be opened outward with a single push.

(2) Fire buckets - Five to ten fire buckets are fully stored with water.

(3) Fire escape - This is necessary for multi-story buildings.
